Spanish Civil War: General Offensive by Both Armies Has Begun; Fierce Fighting Around the Portuguese Border; Government Side Strictly Prevents Internal Treachery

Madrid: According to news from the front line from the special correspondent of this agency, the government army began a general offensive yesterday. Artillery and aircraft bombed the rebel positions, and have not stopped as of now. Infantry advanced under the cover of artillery fire, and made some progress as a result. A team of shock troops has now reached the town of Guadarrama, and another route is advancing towards the Leon Pass via the town of Navacerrada, with support infantry arriving one after another. Fierce fighting is expected there today. Minister of War Salavete recently told the press that the front line situation is extremely smooth. According to news from Sigüenza, the government army captured two rebel cannons and five mortars, and killed a rebel captain and 40 soldiers. (8th, Havas)

Burgos: According to a communiqué recently released by the rebel headquarters in the north, after General Franco, the commander-in-chief of the revolutionary army in the south, arrived in Seville, he immediately ordered an advance towards Madrid, defeating the government armies in Badajoz and Cáceres, capturing many prisoners. One of the senior officers of the government army, Colonel Pu Yi Tang Chai La, was also among those captured, and a large number of military weapons and several armored vehicles were seized. In the north, the revolutionary army is currently increasing troops to various positions, so there is no major battle. Recently, three government army pilots defected with their planes. (8th, Havas)

Madrid: The rebel army is getting closer to the capital city today, and government leaders are therefore very angry with certain countries that are supplying arms to the rebel army, and are increasingly suspicious of government army officers. Former Foreign Minister Fulasige was arrested and imprisoned today, but the charges have not been announced. President Achaana also dismissed the Consul General in New York, and all senior police officers have been dismissed. The socialist mayor of Iskoliyl was imprisoned today, as were 140 monks, and it was announced that the police will search the monasteries. The President appointed General Ligel as commander-in-chief of the Guadarrama army today. (7th, National News Agency)

Front Line of the Rebel Army in Northern Spain: General Mara, commander of the rebel army in the north, told a Associated Press reporter today that the vanguard of the revolutionary army has reached the outskirts of Madrid, and the houses of civilians outside the city are hung with white cloth to indicate neutrality. Government army aircraft bombed villages in this area this morning to prevent the rebel army from advancing. (7th, National News Agency)

Madrid: Fierce fighting is reported to have occurred near Badajoz, Spain, near the border between Portugal and France, and is still ongoing. Both sides are trying to occupy a superior position before launching a major offensive. Rebel leader General Franco is preparing to seize Madrid after succeeding here. The government army defending Badajoz was in danger for several hours due to a mutiny by the city guards. However, after the city guards ran out of bullets, they were suppressed by the republicans. A rebel plane then flew over the city and dropped several heavy bombs on the barracks. It is reported that the barracks have been completely destroyed. Correspondents from Reuters at various centers telegraphed the situation in other parts of Spain as follows: When officials in Malaga sent a telegram to report that the rebel army in Cadiz had surrendered, Madrid was overjoyed. When the Interior Minister continued to announce that "the news of the fall of Cadiz was transmitted too early," the crowd was disappointed again. The French ship Robinson, sailing from Algeciras to Antwerp, was bombed by a plane of unknown nationality five miles from Gibraltar. The bomb fell 220 yards from the ship. The flagship of the British squadron, HMS Douglas, has arrived in Palma, Majorca. The area is currently in the hands of the rebels. It is reported that the government army is currently preparing to launch a major offensive against Palma with twelve seaplanes and 3,200 soldiers collected in Valencia. In addition to four Germans who died in Valencia, three other Germans have met with misfortune in Spain, including a girl. The German government has demanded compensation from the Spanish government for the losses in this unfortunate incident in Valencia. On Menorca, the second largest island in the Balearic Islands, there was a popular uprising against the government. It is reported that no less than 120 rebels were killed, including a naval admiral. (8th, Reuters)

Algeciras: Warships Bombard for a Day; Fortifications Destroyed, Fires Everywhere; British Consul's Wife Hit by Stray Bullet

Algeciras: This area has suffered a day-long bombardment from Spanish government warships, with fires breaking out in many parts of the port. A total of 70 people have died, including one woman and one child, and 60 have been injured. The wife of British Vice-Consul Bagingtai has also been injured. There are many fires within the city, and the power plant has also been destroyed. The circumstances of the British Consul's wife's injury are quite bizarre. When a government warship's shell penetrated the wall of the consulate's reception room, Mr. and Mrs. Bagingtai were talking inside. The roof collapsed from the impact, only injuring the Consul's wife; it can be considered fortunate. (7th National Telegram)

Gibraltar: As a result of the Spanish government warships bombarding Algeciras, the Argentine Consulate has been completely destroyed, and the British Consulate has been hit by two shells, rendering it uninhabitable. One shell exploded inside the building. British Vice-Consul Mr. Bigeonsal and his wife narrowly escaped danger, but Mrs. Bi was slightly injured by falling debris. It is said that her escape was miraculous. All buildings facing the sea had their glass windows and other features shattered beyond recognition, and several houses have been destroyed by shells. It is generally believed that the Spanish government warships have disabled the Algeciras fortifications, as the fortifications fired several rounds but did not retaliate against the warships. It is said that the first shell from the "Jaime I" killed all the gunners on the rebel warship "Taitu", and the remaining sailors immediately abandoned ship and fled, but later returned to the ship and extinguished the fire inside. The "Jaime I", the cruiser "Libertad", and the destroyer "Cervantes" once sailed out to sea, then reappeared in the port this afternoon and bombarded Algeciras, Tarifa, and Ceuta. The "Jaime I" approached the Algeciras harbor and fired continuously. The "Libertad" and "Cervantes" engaged in a mutual bombardment with two rebel seaplanes that arrived from Ceuta, Morocco. While the battle was raging, thirty British residents of Algeciras escaped to Gibraltar by car and arrived safely. A Reuters reporter from Gibraltar traveled to Algeciras by car and saw that almost all the residents had evacuated, and all the houses were locked up. As a result of this bombardment, at least twenty people died and fifty were injured. (8th Reuters Telegram)

Cartagena, Spain: Officers of the Spanish coastal defense gunboat "Jaime I" planned to join the rebels but were detained by the ship's soldiers and have been handed over to the military authorities in Malaga for investigation. The Speaker of the House of Representatives, Barrio, who was previously appointed by the government as Chairman of the Administrative Committee for the Mediterranean coastal provinces, has recently arrived in this port to inspect the defenses. (8th Havas Telegram)

Larache: Several government warships bombarded this area yesterday, firing no less than two hundred rounds. The local losses were heavy, but no shells hit the rebel barracks. All the residents of the city have fled. Seven prisoners also attempted to escape during the chaos, but were shot and killed by the prison guards. (8th Havas Telegram)

Madrid: Cadiz, a port city on the southwestern Atlantic coast of Spain and one of the naval bases, has been in the hands of the rebels since the outbreak of the unrest, along with Algeciras and Huelva. Yesterday, there was a rumor that the port had been recaptured by government troops, but the truth remains to be verified. According to news from Barcelona, semi-official sources there have confirmed this, but news from Malaga states that officials there only claim that government troops have recovered the village of San Fernando near Cadiz, and have not mentioned Cadiz itself. (8th Havas Telegram)

Gibraltar: Air and Sea Forces Clash; Britain Prepares to Take Appropriate Measures

London: Spanish government warships and rebel aircraft have been clashing near the British territory of Gibraltar in recent days. For example, when rebel troops from Spanish Morocco crossed the sea by ship, government warships fired on them. Two shells landed near the Gibraltar racecourse, and two more landed in the harbor. At the same time, rebel aircraft retaliated with bombs, and one large bomb landed in the polo field. It is reported that the British government has protested to both the Spanish government and the rebel authorities, and has instructed the Gibraltar authorities to take all appropriate measures to deal with such incidents if they occur again. (7th Havas Telegram)

London: It was recently stated by responsible sources that the government protested to both the Spanish government and the rebel authorities because the naval and air forces of both sides were fighting in the territorial waters of British Gibraltar, and stray bullets fell into the harbor, endangering British interests. However, neither side was able to prevent this from happening. Therefore, the government decided to protect the dignity of the British flag in Spanish territory on its own. At the same time, regarding the French-proposed non-intervention agreement, the government will continue to work hard to achieve its completion as soon as possible. However, political figures are pessimistic about the prospects of these negotiations, for the following reasons: (A) As far as Germany is concerned, after four members of the youth wing of the Nazi Party in Germany were killed in the village of Sant Martí outside Barcelona, Spain, Germany protested to the Spanish government and demanded that those responsible be punished. If the Madrid government cannot give Germany a satisfactory answer, Germany may also take responsibility for protecting its interests in Spain. This is what political figures fear. Currently, Germany has expressed its support for France's application, but on the condition that the Soviet Union does not aid the Madrid government, and that the German government not only supplies the Spanish rebel General Franco with commercial aircraft, but has also transported a large number of arms and ammunition to support the rebels. If a non-intervention agreement can be concluded quickly, it may be enough to make Germany know its place. Unfortunately, the chances of this agreement being established are very slim. (B) As for Portugal, the only country that has not yet responded to France's application is Portugal. It is said that the Portuguese government intends to make three demands: 1. The neutral status of the port of Tangier in North Africa must be accepted by both sides of the Spanish conflict, as well as other countries. 2. Britain and France must guarantee Portugal's territorial integrity. (C) As for Italy, among the three issues raised by Italy regarding the French proposal, the two concerning the cessation of donations and the adoption of supervisory measures to ensure that all countries uniformly abide by the non-intervention agreement are difficult for all countries to accept. This is also where the obstacles lie. In short, if the non-intervention agreement requires lengthy negotiations and cannot be established quickly, then the situation is urgent and critical, and it is feared that a serious incident may occur before there is time for calm discussion. This is what British people are extremely wary of. (7th Havas Telegram)

Tangier: A Spanish rebel aircraft flew over the Italian mail ship "Dante" at 2:30 PM yesterday. By accident, several of the bombs it was carrying fell near the ship, but fortunately it was not hit. (8th Havas Telegram)

Rebel Leader: Franco Takes New Position, Commands Southern Armies to Advance

Seville: Rebel General Franco has arrived here and plans to organize a revolutionary army to attack Madrid. (8th Reuters Telegram)

Lisbon: It has been confirmed that the leader of the Spanish rebels, General Franco, has crossed the sea from Tetouan, Spanish Morocco, and arrived in the mainland city of Seville. (8th Havas Telegram)

Lisbon: After arriving in Seville from Tetouan, Spanish Morocco, General Franco has taken the position of Commander-in-Chief of all southern armies. All rebel forces in Andalusia, Badajoz, Huelva, and Granada are under his command, in order to launch a major northern expedition and join forces with General Mola's troops in the north to attack the capital, Madrid. In addition, fierce fighting is currently taking place in the province of Badajoz, which borders Portugal. A column led by rebel Colonel Asensio has occupied the city of Mérida, cutting off the transport line between Madrid and Badajoz. It is expected that Badajoz will fall soon. Portuguese troops are currently conducting exercises near the capital to prepare for any eventuality. Furthermore, after serious disturbances occurred on the Portuguese island of Madeira in the Atlantic Ocean yesterday, the government has dispatched four gunboats loaded with troops to the island to cooperate with the original garrison and police to maintain order. The ship "Amelia" has returned from the island, bringing back many rioters who will be tried by a military tribunal organized by the government. (8th Havas Telegram)

Germany Declares to Britain: No Intervention in Spain; Denies Sending More Warships

Berlin: According to well-informed sources here, the German government has currently decided not to actively intervene in the Spanish civil war. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has today received the French government's proposal for non-intervention in Spain, and it is reported that it has accepted it in principle. Semi-official sources here stated today that the German government will make every effort to protect German nationals in Spain, but does not want to encourage a situation in which European countries are divided into two opposing groups of socialists and fascists. However, if German nationals in Spain continue to be harmed or German ships continue to be bombarded, the result will be retaliation by German warships. (8th Reuters Telegram)

London: German Chargé d'Affaires Prince Bismarck visited the Foreign Office today. It is said that he declared to the office that the German government does not intend to take any action in Spain, and denied that German warships have transported ammunition to the Spanish rebels. He also said that Germany does not want to worsen the international situation by providing any assistance to either side in Spain out of political sympathy. In addition, the German Embassy has denied that Ribbentrop, a close confidant of German Chancellor Hitler, advocated sending troops to Barcelona. Political figures believe that after the German diplomatic authorities issued this statement, the situation has become much clearer. This is why the British government, before the governments of Italy, Germany, Belgium, Portugal, Czechoslovakia, Poland, and the Netherlands, will support the French draft of the non-intervention agreement in the Spanish civil war. For example, British Ambassador to Germany Sir Phipps met with German Foreign Minister Neurath last night and stated that the British government urgently wants to see this agreement established. In addition, several British warships are stationed in several Spanish ports to protect British nationals. Regarding the protection of nationals, the British authorities in Gibraltar have also received instructions to prepare to take all effective measures, but joint action with Germany has not been considered. (8th Havas Telegram)

London: The French government today began distributing the plan for non-intervention in the Spanish civil war to various countries, saying that time is of the essence and action must be taken immediately. The one sent to Britain has been delivered today. The French proposal stipulates a ban on the sale of weapons, ammunition, aircraft, warships, and other military supplies to any party in Spain, its Moroccan territories, and all regions under Spanish control. (7th Reuters Telegram)

Berlin: French Ambassador François-Poncet submitted the draft non-intervention agreement in the Spanish civil war proposed by his government to Foreign Minister Neurath. The content lists the specific methods of the non-intervention policy, such as stipulating that the contracting countries shall not sell various military arms, ammunition, military and civilian aircraft, and various warships to Spain. It is reported that Neurath expressed considerable interest in the French proposal. (7th Havas Telegram)

Berlin: Officials here announced today that the German Chargé d'Affaires in Spain has again lodged a serious protest with the Catalan autonomous government, demanding compensation for the murder of four German nationals near Barcelona. It is also understood that Chancellor Hitler is very angry about the anti-German sentiment in Spain, so whether to accept the French proposal for non-intervention in the Spanish civil war is questionable. After Germany protested to the Spanish government, it will send more warships to Spanish territorial waters. (7th National Telegram)

London: Many foreign newspapers claim that the British Vickers-Armstrongs factory is currently supplying a large number of arms to the Spanish government. This afternoon, British officials denied this. It is said that the factory has not obtained an arms export license from the authorities. Without a license, no arms or ammunition can be shipped out of Britain. (7th Reuters Telegram)

Greek Dictatorial Politics: Prime Minister Holds Five Positions; King Sails to Corfu

Athens: After Prime Minister Metaxas adopted a dictatorial system, he concurrently assumed the positions of Minister of Foreign Affairs, Navy, Army, and Air Force. Deputy Prime Minister Savitsa Leos was appointed Minister of Finance, and Skilakakis was appointed Minister of Interior. Today, he led the new cabinet members to King George II to take the oath of office. (8th Havas Telegram)

Athens: King George set off from here last night on a destroyer to Corfu in the Ionian Islands. It is said that he will stay there until mid-September before returning to the capital. It is generally believed that this trip is related to the dictatorial politics of the new Prime Minister Metaxas. Mr. Metaxas stated that he will often go to the various island residences to present official documents for the King to sign. (8th Reuters Telegram)

Belgrade, Yugoslavia: Since Greek Prime Minister Metaxas implemented a dictatorial political system, the various left-wing parties in the country have expressed their opposition. According to news from Athens, the leaders of the country's major political parties, such as Republican leader Cafantaris, Liberal Party leader Papanastasiou, the son of the late People's Party leader Tsaldaris, and Senate Speaker Gonatas, were summoned by King George II today to meet in the palace. They protested against Metaxas's establishment of a dictatorial political system and declared to the King that they were prepared to restore the parliamentary system and organize a nationwide constitutional government. They also said that the various political parties originally supported the monarchy, but since the establishment of the dictatorial political system, their trust in the monarchy has been shaken. Afterwards, the King informed Prime Minister Metaxas of the opinions expressed by the leaders of the various political parties. In addition, Liberal Party right-wing leader Sophoulis refused to attend the audience, saying, "The King personally promised three days ago that he would never allow the establishment of a dictatorial political system. Now, why has he gone back on his word? In my opinion, the King must also bear responsibility." The King then boarded a destroyer at 5:00 PM today to go to Corfu for the summer, planning to stay there until mid-September before returning to the capital. (7th Havas Telegram)

Ministry of Industry Promotes Sweet Potato Planting

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry previously received a case from the Executive Yuan submitted by Li Baohan requesting that the provinces be ordered to actively plant sweet potatoes in order to solve the national food problem. The case was submitted to the Central Agricultural Research Institute for research and discussion. According to the Institute's research report, sweet potato crops are convenient to plant, grow easily, can be used as a side dish or to replace rice and wheat as a staple food, and can be used as a raw material for making alcohol. For the sake of pre-planning for food self-sufficiency and liquid fuel self-sufficiency, promoting planting is essential. According to the report, the Ministry of Industry has issued a notice to the construction departments and social bureaus of each province and city, ordering them to promote planting, and to first engage in sweet potato crop breeding experiments and promote superior varieties, so as to improve quality and increase production. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

Central Mint to Take Over and Reorganize Various Coinage Factories

(Nanjing) In order to unify the right to coin money according to law and to reorganize the old coinage factories, the Ministry of Finance has ordered the custodians of the Hangzhou, Wuchang, Chongqing, Chengdu, and Lanzhou coinage factories to hand over all the factories to the Central Mint for management. It is now understood that the Central Mint has sent personnel to investigate the machine and housing conditions of each factory and will submit a proposed reorganization and application plan to the Ministry of Finance for approval. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

Geological Research Institute Sends Personnel to Jiangxi to Investigate Mineral Resources

Election Lawsuits Can Also Be Under the Jurisdiction of the High Court Branch

(Nanjing) According to Article 58 of the National Assembly Representative Election Law, election lawsuits are under the jurisdiction of the competent High Court and should be tried before other lawsuits, and should be concluded with one trial. Furthermore, Article 20 of the Court Organization Law stipulates that the matters under the jurisdiction of the High Court Branch are the same as those of the High Court. Therefore, the High Court mentioned in the election law can also include the High Court Branch. The above opinion was sent to the General Office of the National Election for review and was approved. The Ministry of Justice issued a notice to all High Courts on the 8th to pay attention to it. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

French Senate Passes Nationalization of Arms Case

(Paris) The Senate recently continued to discuss the government's proposal to nationalize the arms industry. After making slight amendments, it was finally passed. During the discussion, Aviation Minister Gu Te delivered a speech defending the air force part of the case, stating, "After the military aircraft manufacturing plant is nationalized, the government can often increase production efficiency. After the reorganization of the French Air Force, it is hoped that it can have sufficient ordnance. Although I hope that this ordnance will never be used, I also deeply hope that the country will prepare for it as soon as possible, so as to avoid digging a well when thirsty." (8th Havas Dispatch)

(Paris) After the government's proposal to nationalize the arms industry was passed by the Chamber of Deputies, it was immediately submitted to the Senate for discussion. Cabinet Coordinator and Minister of National Defense Dala Di delivered a speech in the Senate yesterday to defend the case. He said, "In order to strengthen national defense, the government does not need to establish a national monopoly system for the arms industry, but should change to national supervision to seek uniformity. This new system is based on the two principles of nationalization and national supervision. Although only a few necessary industries are planned to be nationalized, according to the bill proposed by the government, the Minister of National Defense can exercise supervision over the national arms manufacturing industry and find ways to prevent the activities of certain foreign manufacturers. For various industries preparing for nationalization, the government can add special machinery and hoard a large number of goods in peacetime. All this cannot be done by private manufacturers. When a war breaks out, the country will mobilize, and the national industry can be used for the country's use. Furthermore, in terms of participating soldiers, they all unanimously advocate that the profits obtained by arms merchants from selling arms should be absolutely eliminated in wartime, and should be restricted as much as possible in peacetime. This coincides with the government's bill." (8th Havas Dispatch)

Memoirs of the Emperor of Abyssinia

A Paris newspaper once published the memoirs of the Emperor of Abyssinia. These memoirs were dictated by the Emperor to the French journalist Griolet on a ship to England recently.

In the first part, the Emperor gave a historical account of the period of the struggle for power among the feudal lords. In the second part, the Emperor stated the conspiracy of Italy against Abyssinia, saying: "The most unique thing is that those who declare to the world that my country is not unified are often those who are trying in vain to divide my country. Unfortunately, I do not have the rest of her to describe the full history of the events unfavorable to my neighbors, but I recall the manager of Bagendra, the husband of Queen Sao Di Tou, and the riots of Chief Gugus, which were instigated by the Italians. Not far from the Databo Station is Godal, where Chief Gugus resided. The Italians had a senior nobleman, Borel, there. The residents respected Borel very much because of his old age, and because he legally married an Abyssinian woman and had a very large family. Borel lived according to Abyssinian customs, and therefore maintained close ties with the people. He began to cleverly promote everywhere, saying that the current ruler of the country is Gugus, who is the only one who loves his father and does not allow Europeans to expand his province, and investigates everything about "white culture." According to his opinion, I am neglecting the culture of Abyssinia. Gugus also supported the Italian agent, Duke Franchi Gi. This man also maintained close relations with the Ainu.

When Gugus passed a resolution to start a war against our country, he was killed in the Battle of Kvarara. Twenty years of work by the Italians were turned to ashes by my army in twenty-four hours. Another day I was honored as Emperor, and my coronation ceremony was held in November 1930.

The Ainu chiefs often colluded with the Italians... In 1932, with the help of the Italians, he helped his wife's brother escape and wanted to unite with him to oppose our country. This method failed. The imperial army was ready in a few days. External money failed. However, the Italians never considered themselves defeated. In 1931, they wanted to establish a commercial counselor for the consulate and establish a new consulate in Markos, the capital of Gosa. There is no basis for the existence of such counselors, because no Italian businessman - whether white or black - lives in the area where such counselors are located. We have tolerated it to prove our love, although we know that such counselors are carrying out political propaganda to oppose the establishment of our country."

Next, the Emperor stated the famous Huarwar incident in 1934, when the Italian border guards invaded the Abyssinian border by 120 kilometers and refused to withdraw from this territory. The Emperor continued:

"We have the right to surround the Italian army and take all the methods needed to clear the obvious destruction of our country's territory. However, in order to implement a compromise policy and respect the treaties of the League of Nations and the Italian consul, we have not done so. We want to act in accordance with international law... We know what is happening and demand that we do not stay in the discussion of sovereignty. We firmly believe in our own justice, so we agree to avoid this principled question, and the decision of the arbitration does not place any responsibility on either side. This is our first disappointment."

The third part of the Emperor's memoirs is devoted to the beginning of the Italian-Abyssinian War.

In this part, the Emperor said:

"It is not possible to wage war using European methods. What's more, our military equipment, not only the artillery, but also the machine guns are ridiculous. The northern army operates under various geographical conditions, and every small section of the land can be used as a war position. Its tactics are to conduct guerrilla warfare that makes the enemy feel extremely serious. Only under favorable conditions can the enemy be directly attacked. When the enemy turns to defense, they must retreat. This tactic pursues two major goals: an attitude of cherishing life, because it is recognized that Chen Di's battle can destroy a large number of lives. Secondly, this tactic is intended to keep the enemy constantly tense before the rainy season, when the enemy's military equipment will lose most of its effectiveness.

"This army contacted the Italians later. I once ordered Chief Gugus's army to occupy 50 kilometers of the border, and ordered Chief Sem's army to occupy 80 kilometers from the railway. I firmly believed that the neutral zone should be observed by the League of Nations, and it has indeed been observed. It is not easy to explain this position to the Abyssinian people. They thought this was the first territorial concession. When the enemy's actions have reached a serious level, it is also difficult to make the Abyssinian people believe that they must retreat. Even such a valuable person as Chief Sem also withdrew from Aduwa in tears, and as a result, everyone knew what I was expecting, and all fought under the slogan of "cleaning up internal traitors." Perhaps this over-caution has failed. However, we can never predict that the disparity in military equipment will not cause fear among our people...

Gugus's rebellion was not the result of pro-Italianism. This is the only chance for the rebellion, and at the same time, the second-rate officers proved that the Abyssinian people will never conspire with foreigners. Gugus was acting under the shadow of fear. His carpenters also estimated the great superiority of Italian military equipment. Lack of experience has weakened their belief in the resilience of their own soldiers. Heavy profits and high salaries have played an extra role.

"The Italians once estimated the so-called rebellion of the Abyssinian people in 'Tritribery'. It is said that the Abyssinian people in the provinces of Barummiel and Gosham were selected by the Italians as soldiers in the Tritribia War. After serving the Italians for ten or five years, they were sent back to their hometowns. However, the fact is that these 'Tritribery' people have received good training and education, and are the most determined and outstanding anti-Italian fighters. These people often express dissatisfaction when they come back from serving in the Italian army, because they are given the most dangerous work, but they are not given the scheduled rewards... The details of the Hauner incident are well known, so there is no need to repeat them. However, the incident in the south caused by the large-scale Italian invasion of Niger is still little known... This kind of Italian advancement is only because Chief Kista wanted to attack Doro and broke into Italian Somaliland. During a considerable period, there were 15,000 to 20,000 troops who had broken away from the base by 400 kilometers and were using cargo trucks to supply their food. The enemy's air force caused Chief Kista to retreat and lost contact with the base, and was bombed by the enemy. The Italian air force destroyed the medicine storage, causing the Kista army to lose the necessary medicines for treating fever and disease, and diseases spread in this area. When the connection with the base was established, Chief Kista had stopped retreating, and at that time, enemy aircraft were bombing residents on the transportation road."

In the fourth and fifth parts of his memoirs, the Emperor recounted the activities of the Italian Air Force. He said that because most of the terrain is mountainous, Italian planes fly very high, which is why the Abyssinian people shot down very few planes (18 planes). However, for this reason, Italian planes fly very high, making it easier for the Abyssinian people to defend themselves. The Emperor also said:

"The route of the plane seems very far away. Our lookout posted on all the mountain peaks, with the help of all the bushes, warns our army of the danger in the sky. This activity is very good. An army of 10,000 to 20,000 people is always hidden, without a trace... When the Italian pilots have seen this, they begin to bomb all the wooded areas, but without any effect. So Italian pilots were ordered to bomb the churches, as if our people were hiding there. From a military point of view, this is the most cruel and pointless act. Women, children and the elderly died under the ruins of the collapsed walls. Every church has a library, and some of the documents contained therein are the only evidence of antiquity, precious in science, literature, and art... I don't need to talk about the paintings that decorate these churches... For example, Dunbianni, especially Xier, the treasures lost there can never be recovered."

The Emperor continued—

"The air force usually used to deal with the Abyssinian people has not been very effective... Therefore, the Italian General Staff decided to end the military before the rainy season. The new tactics of the Italians are as follows: they often use poison gas and choose residents far away from the positions as targets for attack. At the beginning of the war, the Italians used tear gas bombs... The Abyssinian people immediately adapted to this point and dispersed when attacking. Changes in the wind direction rendered this gas ineffective. The Italians had used a kind of chlorine at this time, but it was very primitive. They dropped small buckets full of this liquid from the plane. Very few people were in these small buckets. The number of victims is limited, and the infected area is also limited... Then the Italian General Staff, fearing the failure of the Makaer raid and that the Italians had been driven out of Xier, decided to adopt another method of chemical warfare, which no country can resist without the necessary self-defense technology. The plane is equipped with a sprayer... Each plane has nine, fifteen, eighteen planes in groups, with each other The distance is such that the mist sprayed by each aircraft can form a large mist with the mist sprayed by other aircraft... It has been extended for several days since January 1926. Anyone who hits this kind of chlorine raindrop, and those who drink poisoned water, suffer from severe eczema. Only thatched huts or jungles can avoid it. In a country with lush trees and greenery, people cannot touch things with their hands, because death is everywhere. Corpses can be found everywhere... This poisonous gas immediately spread throughout the country. In the past, the Abyssinian people said they were fighting with people and believed in their own strength. However, when the Abyssinian people started to use tools that they considered inhuman, they began to believe that they were fighting with demons." (External Theory Society)

Situation in Eastern Sui Suddenly Becomes Tense, One Side Targets Shanxi and Suiyuan, Rebel Army Advances Are Repelled

Beiping Correspondence, The situation in eastern Sui is becoming increasingly tense, and the authorities in Shanxi and Suiyuan have also been paying attention to it for a long time. Unexpectedly, on July 30th and the 2nd of this month, the rebel army of Li Shouxin, along with the bandits in northern Chahar, did invade. Although they were all defeated, this incident has aroused the attention of all parties, because this is a move by Li's rebels with a background.

Since a certain party has coveted Inner Mongolia, the so-called re-creation of the "Mongolia State" and "Dayuan State" have been widely publicized. Subsequently, the "eastern Hebei" and "northern Chahar" issues have occurred one after another. That is, a certain party has a planned chronic invasion action. Therefore, after repeated negotiations, there has been no effect. After the fall of the six counties in northern Chahar, the puppet army has successively arrived. The automobile road and the airport have also been built. After the plan is completed, they will force De Wang to recruit Mongolian soldiers and expand their strength as a vanguard. The current formation has three divisions, all under the command of Li's rebels Shouxin.

The military plan of a certain party is to first occupy eastern Sui, then advance into the provincial capital of Suiyuan, and capture northern Shanxi. If a certain party realizes this plan, Hebei and Chahar will be easily obtained. Therefore, its target has turned to Shanxi and Suiyuan. The advancing troops are divided into three layers. The bandits are the vanguard, the puppet Mongolian army is in the middle, and the army of a certain country is in the last team. Currently, two regiments of soldiers from a certain country have arrived in Zhangbei County, Chahar Province. The airport built by a certain country in Shangdu has also been completed. Li Shouxin is now in Shangdu coordinating everything. In addition, a certain puppet Manchu guerrilla commander went to Tianjin at the beginning of this month. At that time, Yin Rugeng also went to Tianjin from Tong County to secretly discuss changing the security teams of Zhang Qingyu, Zhang Yantian, Li Yunsheng, and Zhao Lei in the war zone into guerrillas, divided into eight teams, and preparing to send a part to northern Chahar to assist in the invasion of eastern Sui. The authorities are paying close attention to this.

On July 30th, several hundred bandits, in the name of the puppet border defense self-defense army,窜entered from northern Chahar and harassed Tumuer Tai, which belongs to Taolin County, Suiyuan Province. The local militia resisted from the fort and fought each other for several hours. The bandits were unable to support and began to retreat towards Shangdu. On the 2nd of this month, the bandits came again and participated in the puppet army to move forward together. The number increased from several hundred to more than two thousand people. They attacked Honggen Ertu, which belongs to Taolin County, and clashed with the cavalry company of Zhao Chengshou's troops stationed there, resulting in a fierce battle. The bandits attacked for two days without success, with casualties of one to two hundred people. At this time, Zhao Chengshou also arrived at Pingdi Quan and sent Peng Brigade Commander to lead cavalry to reinforce the area. At the same time, Damilingsulong, the General Manager of the Inner Mongolia Zheng Huang Banner, also volunteered to lead troops to assist. The bandits were all seriously injured and retreated dozens of miles to the east. In the past three days, the situation in eastern Sui has been calm, and the bandits have not committed any more crimes. The public believes that a certain country has not yet formally launched, so the future problem may inevitably expand. (7th)

National Children's Welfare Conference: First General Meeting Held, Approving Various Safeguarding and Relief Proposals

Qingdao Correspondence: The Second National Children's Welfare Conference held its first general meeting at 10:30 AM on the 6th. All representatives participated. First, the General Secretary, Chen Tiesheng, reported on the representatives who had arrived later from various places. It was decided that Chairman Zhao Jinqing would report on: (1) the agenda for the day; (2) the reports to be reviewed by each group; and (3) the election of exhibition evaluation committee members. Then, Liu Tingfang lectured on the philosophy of children's welfare, finishing at 11:00 AM. Immediately afterward, the Safeguarding and Relief groups, having completed their review, presented their reports. After discussion by the entire body, it was decided to adopt the revised opinions based on the review. The remaining groups are to be presented to the general meeting for discussion after their review is completed. Finally, it was decided to elect exhibition evaluation committee members by nomination. The meeting adjourned at 12:30 PM. In the evening at 8:00 PM, in addition to those groups that had not completed their review continuing their work, a lecture meeting was held at the venue.

The following proposals were passed at the first general meeting: (A) Safeguarding Group: (1) Based on the resolutions of the previous session, to request the government once again to safeguard children's welfare undertakings and support their development. Review opinion: Submitted to the general meeting for review and implementation. Resolution: Passed. (2) To request the Ministry of Interior to petition the Executive Yuan to issue a nationwide order strictly prohibiting traditional midwifery practices to protect infant lives. Review opinion: Request the general meeting to refer this case to the Health Group for joint handling. Resolution: Passed. (3) To request the general meeting to find ways to protect the Yongchun Poor People's Hospital. Review opinion: Regarding children's welfare undertakings, another case has already been submitted. It is proposed that this case not be considered. (5) To petition the government to strictly prohibit child brides to maintain humanity and strengthen the nation's foundation. Review opinion: Petition the Executive Yuan to reiterate the prohibition based on the National Government's decree banning child brides. The association should separately notify various children's welfare organizations to conduct detailed investigations and provide effective relief. Resolution: Passed. (6) To petition the Executive Yuan to strictly prohibit troops from stationing in charitable institutions to avoid harassment. Review opinion: It has been found that the military administration department has already issued a ban on stationing troops in charitable organizations. However, the reality of troops being stationed in various places still exists. It is proposed that the association petition the Executive Yuan to reiterate the previous order. Resolution: Passed. (7) To establish child protection agencies. Review opinion: After the conclusion of Children's Year, it is heard that the central government intends to organize a Children's Happiness Committee and establish branch associations in various provinces and cities as a permanent undertaking. It is found that this coincides with the opinion of this case. It is proposed that the general meeting petition the Executive Yuan to find ways to facilitate its early realization. Resolution: Passed. (8) To propose that the general meeting send a letter to the Shaanxi Provincial Government, etc., to issue a notice to protect the Yulin Infant Asylum. Review opinion: Proposed to be handed over to the Children's Welfare Association for review. Resolution: Passed. (9) To request the prohibition of keeping and abusing maids to save unfortunate girls. (10) To request the cessation of maltreatment of young performers to respect humanity. (11) To request the relief of apprentices' suffering. (12) To request the rescue of infant prostitutes' lives to respect humanity. Review opinion: The above four cases are to be combined and handled with the fifth case. (13) To eliminate traditional midwives and replace them with formally trained personnel to protect the lives of mothers and newborns. Review opinion: To be merged with the second case for handling. Resolution: Passed. (B) Relief Group: (1) To have the general meeting petition the Ministry of Interior to issue a nationwide order to all provinces, cities, and counties to uniformly expand or establish orphanages and infant asylums to broaden relief efforts. Review opinion: The general meeting should petition the National Government to issue a nationwide order to all provinces, cities, and counties to handle the case as proposed. Resolution: Passed. (2) To widely establish infant asylums to provide relief to poor children in various places. Review opinion: The general meeting should forward this to the Chinese Children's Welfare Association and send a letter requesting the local authorities to pay special attention to infant matters or establish relief agencies to provide remedies. Resolution: Passed. (3) Privately established children's welfare organizations that have been operating for many years with excellent results but are financially strained and unable to expand their enrollment should be granted government funding to expand their enrollment and broaden relief efforts. Review opinion: The general meeting should petition the National Government to handle the case as proposed. Resolution: Passed. (4) To petition the Executive Yuan to instruct the Ministry of Interior to expand the scope of children admitted to relief homes and orphanages in various places to provide universal relief. Review opinion: The general meeting should petition the Ministry of Interior to delete the word "dependent" from Article 20 of Chapter 3 of the Relief Home Organization Regulations to broaden relief efforts. Resolution: Passed as amended. (5) To request the National Government to instruct local governments in all provinces to prepare funds for the relief of poor children to expand relief efforts. Review result: The general meeting should petition the National Government to instruct local governments in all provinces to handle the case as proposed. Resolution: Passed. (6) To request the National Government to instruct local governments in all provinces and cities to universally establish children's relief agencies to broadly foster poor children. Review opinion: The general meeting should petition the National Government to instruct local governments in all provinces and cities to handle the case as proposed. (7) To request that all children's welfare institutions and organizations nationwide pay attention to the lives of poor children and actively provide relief to prevent them from going astray. Review opinion: Send a letter to the General Meeting Secretariat to forward it to the Education and Training Group for review. Resolution: Passed. (8) How should homeless children in society be rescued? Review opinion: To be merged with the Education and Training Group for joint handling. Resolution: Passed. (9) Independent children's relief agencies should be widely established nationwide, and attention should be paid to education and training methods. Review opinion: The general meeting should petition the National Government to instruct all provinces and cities to establish relief agencies. Resolution: Passed. (10) What preparations should be made for rescuing children in times of emergency? Review opinion: Jointly reviewed with the Administrative Group. Resolution: Passed. (11) Relief for disabled children. Review opinion: The general meeting should petition the National Government to instruct local governments in all provinces to establish relief agencies. Resolution: Passed. (12) Regarding petitioning the highest administrative authorities to fix relief funds to prevent children from becoming displaced. Review opinion: To be merged with the Administrative Group for further review. Resolution: Passed. (13) To request that the administrative heads of each province instruct the mayors and county magistrates to vigorously support relief efforts to promote development. Review opinion: The general meeting should petition the National Government to instruct local governments to issue protection orders. Resolution: Passed. (August 6th)

Tianjin Public Security Bureau: Cracking Down on a Major Drug Manufacturing Center, Arresting Ten Japanese Nationals and One Chinese National, Seizing Drugs Worth Over 300,000 Yuan

Tianjin Correspondence: The Tianjin Municipal Public Security Bureau recently received a confidential report stating that a large-scale drug manufacturing center was located in the Fifth District of the Sixth District of the city, managed by a certain foreign national. On the 5th, the bureau ordered its subordinates and notified the Japanese police station to conduct a raid. The main suspects, manufacturing equipment, and stored products were all transported to the Japanese police station. The entire case is currently under interrogation. The details of the incident are recorded below.

Organization

At No. 27 Machang Road, located in the Fifth District of the Sixth District of this city, a high-rise building stands, which is the private property of Zhang Huaizhi's younger brother, Zhang Huaibin. The area occupied is no less than several tens of acres, with approximately 40 rooms inside the building. The space remained vacant for many days. Last month, a Chinese man named Wang Yaozu rented the building for a monthly rent of 250 yuan, claiming to organize a "Ping An Transportation Company". They moved in on the 27th of last month and began operations. Japanese nationals frequently entered and exited the premises, and security was unusually tight. There were many suspicious aspects, which attracted the attention of the authorities. After a thorough investigation by Li Zhiping, the captain of the Second Detective Team of the Public Security Bureau, it was discovered that the Ping An Company was indeed a major drug manufacturing center, with a cost of several hundred thousand yuan.

Crackdown

After receiving the report, Li deemed the case important and reported the situation to Director Cheng on the morning of the 5th. Cheng immediately dispatched the Chief of the Security Corps, Tong Zexian, the Chief Inspector, Wang Dianchen, the Chief of the Detective Corps, Yang Enhua, and Captain Li Zhiping, along with officers Chen Chaozhen, Team Leader Tian Jixiang, Squad Leaders Chen Bingheng and Tang Zhenshan, and officers Yang Xiupu and others. They notified the Japanese police station and, with the cooperation of Department Chief Matsushita and special agents Li Zizhen and Zhang Baoting, rode in armored vehicles to the reported location, surrounding the No. 27 building. After knocking on the door for a long time, it seemed that the people inside were aware of the situation and refused to open the door. The team leaders of the Second Team, Tian Jixiang and Tang Zhenshan, used soft ladders to climb over the surrounding wall and bravely jumped down.

Capture

After the door was opened, the officers entered the courtyard and searched each room. A total of ten Japanese suspects were arrested: Watanabe Saburo, Kondo Kanetaro, Itabashi Tomihira, Matsumoto Genichi, Kakuda Yoshiyuki, Nakajima, Mukai Sakue, Suda, Nakamura, and others. One Chinese national, Wang Yaozu, was arrested, and the Chinese ringleader, Li Yurong, escaped. At the scene, 16 vats of manufactured heroin, 12 motors and air conditioners, 3 electric rollers, more than 10 glass filter tubes, and 17 drying vats (filled with unrefined opium paste) were seized, as well as approximately tens of thousands of taels of processed opium and five large packages of white powder, with a total value of over 300,000 yuan. The Japanese side, due to the inconvenience of carrying the opium paste in the drying vats, poured it all into the ditch. All items were loaded onto four heavy trucks, along with the ten Japanese suspects, and transported back to the Japanese police station.

Confession

The Chinese national, Wang Yaozu, was taken back to the Second Team by Captain Li. According to Wang Yaozu's confession, he is 26 years old, a native of this city, and resides in Chentang Zhuangzi. The Ping An Company was moved from Huayuan Street in the Japanese Concession. He is currently working as a cook at the Ping An Company. The fugitive Li Yurong is in charge of running errands. His confession was extremely cunning. However, according to inquiries made by the team to the rental agency, all rental procedures were handled by Wang Yaozu, which proves that Wang is one of the main culprits. The Japanese side stated at the time that the drug den may have been operated by Japanese ruffians and should be subject to Japanese legal judgment. All drugs should be destroyed by the Japanese side. Director Cheng Xixian yesterday ordered Officer Chen Chaozhen to take a formal letter to the Japanese side requesting extradition. Chen returned to the team at 8:30 PM, and it was heard that the result was satisfactory. (6th)

Gansu Province County Farmers' Association Organization: Only One Level Below the County, Land Administration Bureau Handles Registration

Lanzhou Correspondence: Yu Xuezhong, Chairman of the Gansu Provincial Government, stated that the administrative regions of the province's counties were previously divided into several townships. Recently, townships were changed to districts. The so-called "district" is in the same position as the former township. The Farmers' Association Law stipulates that the township farmers' association below the county is now the district farmers' association below the county. However, the name "district" is easily confused with the name of the urban districts below the city. It is now proposed to instruct each county that those using the name "district farmers' association" should still be changed to "township farmers' association". The area of the farmers' association can be specified in the charter. In the southeastern provinces, due to dense populations, most places often have two levels of organization below the county: district and township, with the district being the higher-level farmers' association above the township. The previous instructions to the counties on organizational procedures also stipulated two levels of district and township below the county. However, observing the situation in this province, where the land is vast and the population is sparse, the so-called township in most counties (i.e., the township in the countryside) has households numbering less than several dozen. It is more appropriate to adopt only one level of township below the county. It is proposed that the district farmers' association level in the previously issued organizational procedures not be stipulated. Special instructions are given to each county to comply with this and are communicated to the provincial party headquarters.

The Provincial Land Administration Bureau was previously ordered to conduct registration of urban land in the provincial capital, which was supposed to be completed within four months. However, since this was the first time this had been done, the people were mostly hesitant to apply for property rights. Even those who had applied had incomplete procedures and required personnel to investigate to ensure accuracy. Verifying deeds and going back and forth took time. It coincided with the agricultural production season, and many people went out of the city to harvest. After more than three months, only half of the property owners had applied. If done hastily, not only would the people not be able to cope, but there would also be concerns that the office staff would make omissions. In addition, the provincial and municipal land must be measured using triangulation to comply with regulations. Therefore, it was difficult to complete the task within the four-month limit. The bureau requested the provincial government to extend the deadline by two months to expedite the work and ensure thoroughness. It is now learned that the provincial government, after receiving the report, has approved the request and ordered that the work be expedited.

Songjiang: City River Dredging Completed

The city river in the urban and suburban areas of this county was extensively dredged last year. Due to time constraints, the third section, from the Xiwai Water Gate Bridge to the Taoxing Bridge, was left unfinished. This section is the most prosperous commercial area, with densely packed residences. The riverbed was severely silted up. Therefore, the county government re-measured and planned to dredge the river, entrusting the First District Office to handle it. The district solicited bids, and Wu Xinji won the bid to undertake the project. The dredging was done in sections. The section from the Taoxing Bridge to the Malu Bridge was completed earlier, inspected, and the dam was opened for water flow. The completion of the sections from the Malu Bridge to the Chang Bridge and to the Xiwai Water Gate Bridge was originally scheduled for the 20th of last month. However, due to continuous heavy rain, water accumulated within the dam, requiring additional pumping. The project was quite large, causing a delay until yesterday. Merchants and residents urgently requested that the county government send personnel to inspect and accept the project and open the dam as soon as possible, as water was urgently needed in the summer. Magistrate Li, considering the situation, believed it to be true and immediately appointed the chief of the Third Section, Chen Xibin, to conduct an on-site inspection of the dredged river sections. The chief of the First District, Shen Fuyun, and the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, Cheng, supervised the inspection, which was completed and opened at 9:00 AM today.

Kunshan: Conducting Citizen Oaths

The county-wide citizen oath registration has been earnestly handled by each district, which has instructed its affiliated township offices to do so. Each township has now set the dates for citizen oath registration from the 6th to the 10th. In recent days, a large number of citizens have gone to the registration offices to take the oath. Each district office must compile the name lists and report them to the county government by the 15th for the issuance of citizen certificates.

Discovery of a Turtle with a Human Face

This county has recently been plagued by continuous rain, causing deep water accumulation in the fields. On the afternoon of the 7th, Shen A-san, a farmer near Qingyang Port, discovered a turtle about eight inches long while working in the field after the rain. The turtle was unusually active in the field. Upon closer inspection, he found patterns resembling a mouth, nose, eyes, and hair on its back, exactly like a human face. A-san was very surprised upon seeing this and urgently called the surrounding farmers to observe. All believed it to be an ominous sign and immediately killed the turtle and threw it into the river.

Suzhou: Preparing for Zhang Taiyan's State Funeral

After Zhang Taiyan passed away in Suzhou, the central government decided to hold a state funeral and appointed a preparatory committee. According to news from the funeral committee, Mr. Zhang's coffin will be buried in Hangzhou. Mrs. Zhang, Feng Guoli, visited Hangzhou once to inspect the burial site. The committee members will hold a meeting in Suzhou in early September to discuss matters related to the funeral. Jinfan Road, where Mr. Zhang's residence is located, was newly built last year and has no streetlights. The electric company has decided to install streetlights on the road within days to facilitate traffic, as the funeral is approaching. The funeral date is scheduled for mid-October.

Recovering Huge Sums from Opium Paste Merchants

The Lao Qiaoxing and other three opium paste merchants in Suzhou secretly increased opium prices, illegally collecting over 70,000 yuan in profits. The Provincial Anti-Opium Association learned of this and confirmed the facts. The county was ordered to recover the 70,000 yuan in illegal profits in full. The three opium paste merchants argued that the opium price increase was approved by the County Anti-Opium Association and was not a private increase, requesting exemption from payment. The province did not approve this and ordered the county to thoroughly recover the funds. Magistrate Deng, acting on the order, set a deadline of five days for each opium paste merchant to submit the full amount. The opium paste merchants were granted a three-day extension, which expires on the 10th. If the funds are not raised by the deadline, Magistrate Deng will implement the enforcement order, requiring the guarantors of each opium paste merchant to compensate the full amount. However, the opium paste merchants believe the amount is too large and are finding it difficult to raise the funds. In addition, the anti-opium committee members Zhang Yipeng and Liu Yun have been impeached by the Supervisory Envoy's Office, and Zhang and others have submitted a request for disposition.

Changshu: New Court Selects Site

The Jiangsu High Court has included the issue of establishing a local court in this area in the budget for the 25th year of the Republic, making it certain to happen. Regarding the location, the Rule of Law Promotion Association advocates for renting the old county government buildings from the Hui family for continued use. The President of the High Court specially dispatched Secretary Shi Hanyun to Changshu to survey the site. As a result, it was determined that the old county government buildings were too old, difficult to repair, and reconstruction might conflict with private property. Therefore, it was considered that the New City God Temple (Zhaowen Temple) was the most suitable, and repairs and reconstruction could be determined based on the available funds. According to the county magistrate's opinion, it is proposed that the current county government be vacated and rebuilt at the library site, but requiring a subsidy of 20,000 yuan from the High Court. Secretary Shi has returned to Suzhou for instructions. If this is realized, the Changshu Local Court can be established within this year.

Public Security Bureau Chief Transferred

Zhou Ding, the chief of the Public Security Bureau in this area, has held the position for two years. Recently, the provincial government decided in a meeting to transfer Zhou to the provincial government for appointment. Chen Yuchu, who was originally the chief of the Wuxi County Public Security Bureau, will be transferred to Changshu to succeed him. It is scheduled that Director Chen will come to Changshu on the 9th to take over and assume duties.

Wuxi: Public Security Bureau Chief Changed

Chen Yuchu, the chief of the Public Security Bureau in this county, received an order on the 7th to be transferred to the Public Security Bureau of Changshu. The vacancy will be filled by Zhang Da, the chief of the Public Security Bureau of Kunshan County. After receiving the news, Director Chen instructed his departments to complete the handover on the 8th and personally went to the province for instructions.

Nantong: Water Recedes from Reclaimed Cotton Fields

The Jiangbei coastal reclaimed area previously suffered from drought, but in the past half month, the weather changed, and heavy rain poured down. The low-lying fields of various companies became flooded. Fortunately, the weather has been clear for several days, and the water has drained quickly. The cotton seedlings in the reclaimed area have grown even better after this heavy rain.

Busting a Drug Den in the Eastern Suburbs

The detective team of the Nantong County Public Security Bureau busted a secret drug den selling drugs in the central town of the eastern suburbs on the morning of the 7th. Morphine was seized, and Sun Maoqi, Gu Guide, and Dong Liu, among others, were arrested on the spot and sent to the District Security Command for interrogation.

Gaoyou: Lu Chen Grain Stores Resuming Business

The 45 Lu Chen grain stores outside the South Gate of this county closed down entirely due to the proposed increase of 0.5% in business tax by Zang Langxuan, director of the Business Tax Bureau, starting from August 1st. The stores believed that this would have a significant impact, and it was not implemented in neighboring counties. The closure lasted for three days, from the 2nd to the 4th, affecting the livelihoods of thousands of people. Xu Lianqing, Wang Weibai, and other standing committee members of the County Chamber of Commerce, in view of this, came forward on the 5th to mediate, initially collecting taxes at the old rate. They waited for Chairman Wang Hongzao to return to You and negotiate improvements with Director Zang. In the afternoon, the Grain Guild vigorously persuaded all the grain stores to resume business. However, due to the rainy weather, transactions were slow.

Extreme Damage to Piled Wheat

In the past ten days, this county has experienced continuous rain, and the large amount of wheat purchased in You by factories and firms in Shanghai and Tianjin could not be shipped out in time, piling up in the warehouses. As a result, it has become moldy and suffered extreme damage. Nan Mao Xin alone lost 60,000 to 70,000 shi of wheat. Other companies and firms have also lost 20,000 to 30,000 shi each.

Huzhou: Car Drives Into the Lake

The third passenger car on the Hangzhou-Changxing Road, carrying five passengers, departed from Hangzhou at noon on the 6th. At around 2:00 PM, the car reached the Yingshi Tomb near the Huzhou station. Due to the heavy rain in recent days, the water in the lake was level with the shore. The driver, due to a moment of carelessness, drove the car into the lake. After hearing the news, the Huzhou station immediately sent people to rescue the six passengers and the driver, sending them to the Gospel Hospital for treatment. After entering the hospital, three passengers were discharged immediately because they were not injured. The other three were also slightly injured and remained in the hospital for treatment. It is believed that there is no danger.

Haizhou: One Bomb Kills Twelve People

Jia Xingbang, an ironworker from the Ye Hai area on the border between Muyang and Suqian counties, usually sets up a furnace to cast and sell plowshares (i.e., farming tools) to meet the needs of rural areas. However, the materials he used were mostly scrap tin and old iron, etc., because the cost was lower. In the spring of this year, Jia went to Muyang County to buy scrap iron. He did not know that someone mistakenly sold several discarded bombs from the former 25th Route Army under the Tianhou Palace dam at a low price. Jia, tempted by the small profit, bought several bombs and carried them home. Initially, he planned to put them in the furnace to melt them for plowshares. Later, someone who knew about it said that there was gunpowder inside, which was too dangerous, and advised him to stop. However, Jia had exchanged money for the bombs and could not bear to throw them away, so he placed them at home and still wanted to find a way to take out the powder and melt it in the furnace. When Jia lit the furnace at noon the day before yesterday, he suddenly remembered the bombs he had previously stored at home, so he took them out and played with them, but he still dared not touch the fuse. Coincidentally, a neighbor, Chen, who had been an artilleryman for many years, was on the scene and claimed to have considerable experience in this area and was willing to remove the fuse. Jia was overjoyed and handed him iron pliers. Chen did not hesitate and used the pliers to remove the bomb's fuse. The crowd avoided each other to prevent an explosion. After a while, he successfully removed the fuse and threw the bomb on the ground. The crowd gathered again, no longer afraid because the previous bomb had been handled successfully. Everyone was watching closely to see how to use the pliers to remove the fuse. Unexpectedly, just as he was shaking the pliers, white smoke suddenly billowed out of the fuse. The crowd knew something was wrong and fled, but with a deafening sound, the bomb exploded, with bodies and bones flying all over the sky. Some had no limbs left, others had their heads blown off, and some had only one arm remaining. Chen, who was using the pliers on the bomb, had no remains left. It is estimated that twelve people were killed and four were seriously injured. It can be said to be a tragedy.

Local News

Preparing for Citizen Registration and Oath-Taking: City Government Issues Regulations for Citizen Registration and Oath-Taking; National Assembly Election Office to Convene a Meeting of Various Agencies

Citizen registration and oath-taking are fundamental conditions for obtaining any voting or eligibility rights in the National Assembly elections. Therefore, since the preparations for the National Assembly election have begun, citizen registration and oath-taking cannot be delayed or postponed. Given the unique local circumstances of this city, its dense population, and its status as a special district, in order to ensure rapid and efficient implementation, meticulous research is required based on official regulations. Consequently, the preparation process has been relatively time-consuming. According to news from the Municipal National Assembly Election Office, regarding this matter, the Municipal Government issued Instruction No. 19716 yesterday, promulgating the regulations. The office, recognizing the urgency, has decided to proceed expeditiously and has scheduled a meeting for relevant agencies and organizations at 10:00 AM on the 12th of this month to discuss all matters, in order to commence the process as soon as possible. The original text of the government instruction and regulations are recorded below:

Municipal Government Instruction

Shanghai Municipal Government Instruction No. 19716, issued to the Shanghai Municipal Representative Election Office for the National Assembly, states: Regarding the matter of citizen oath-taking and registration in this city, the Ministry of Interior has previously responded by telegram, instructing the Public Security Bureau to consult with your office on its implementation. We have duly issued instructions accordingly. As a result of consultations, a set of "Regulations for Citizen Registration and Citizen Oath-Taking in Shanghai Municipality" has been formulated to provide a basis for implementation. In addition to instructing the Public Security Bureau to assist your office in accordance with these regulations, a copy of the regulations is hereby issued to you for compliance. This instruction is issued.

Original Text of Regulations

Regulations for Citizen Registration and Citizen Oath-Taking in Shanghai Municipality: 1. Citizens of this city shall, in accordance with the legal age (20 years or older), fulfill citizen registration and citizen oath-taking (members of organizations shall have their organizations handle this on their behalf). 2. Citizen registration and citizen oath-taking in this city shall be conducted by district, according to the former administrative divisions (17 urban and rural areas) and two special districts. Each district shall be further divided into several locations for processing, based on the distance of roads and the density of households. 3. Due to the dense population and vast area of this city, it is impossible to complete citizen registration as scheduled without the joint efforts of all agencies and organizations. Therefore, the following agencies and organizations are designated to be responsible for implementation: (A) Municipal Party Headquarters and District Party Headquarters, (B) Boy Scouts Council, (C) Defense Committee, (D) Public Security Bureau, (E) Education Bureau, (F) Education Association, (G) Municipal Farmers' Association, (H) Municipal Federation of Trade Unions. 4. Although citizen registration in this city will be conducted jointly by various agencies and organizations, a system of division of labor and responsibility will be adopted to ensure smooth operations. Each organization will be responsible for designated areas. The allocation table will be determined separately. 5. The procedures for citizen registration and citizen oath-taking are as follows: A. The organization or agency responsible for an area shall distribute citizen registration forms to all residents in the area according to the prescribed date, instructing them to fill them out and keep them. B. Residents shall fill out the forms according to the prescribed date and submit them to the designated citizen oath-taking location, where they will take the oath simultaneously. C. At the oath-taking location, the oath administrator shall verify the citizen's registration form for errors and instruct them to make corrections, and then have them perform the oath-taking procedure. D. The oath administrator shall organize the citizen registration forms and oaths and submit them to the Municipal Election Office to create citizen certificates. E. After the citizen certificates are created, they will be distributed, or citizens will be instructed to collect them themselves. F. After the deadline for citizen registration and citizen oath-taking, the Election Office shall announce the results by district. If there are any omissions in issuance or registration, citizens in all areas shall be allowed to complete registration and take the oath on a designated date, limited to one day. G. The organization or agency responsible for distributing registration forms in a certain district shall report the name of its person in charge, the total number of team members, and the number of teams formed to the office for record-keeping. H. These regulations shall be implemented upon approval by the Municipal Election Supervisor.

Scheduled Meeting

The National Assembly Election Office yesterday sent letters to the Municipal Party Headquarters, District Party Headquarters, Defense Committee, Boy Scouts Council, Public Security Bureau, Education Bureau, Education Association, Municipal Farmers' Association, Federation of Trade Unions, etc., stating: Regarding the matter of citizen registration and oath-taking in this city, the Municipal Government has issued regulations to our office. We have scheduled a meeting of all organizations and agencies at 10:00 AM on the 12th of this month at our office, No. 107 Fenglin Bridge Municipal Government, to discuss all matters in order to facilitate implementation. In addition to sending separate letters, we hereby request your office to investigate and ensure that representatives are sent to attend at that time.

Applying to the Jianghai Customs: Deadline for Registration and Licensing Approaching - Limited to the 11th of This Month; Failure to Obtain License Will Affect Freight Transportation

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce's Anti-Smuggling Committee held its fourth executive committee meeting yesterday. Attendees included Ge Jiecun, Luo Qinghua, Yang Guanbei, Dong Zihua, Ge Weian, etc. The meeting was chaired by Ge Jiecun. The following cases were discussed: (1) Public associations for the candy and biscuit industry, silk industry, northern and southern goods exchange industry, transit industry, new drug industry, and woolen industry reported the establishment of anti-smuggling branches and submitted their regulations for record-keeping. The meeting resolved to approve the record-keeping. (2) The case of supplementing the deputy leaders of the inspection and communication groups was discussed. The meeting resolved to supplement Gan Tinghui as the deputy leader of the inspection group and Liu Minzhai as the deputy leader of the communication group. (3) The paper industry proposed to find a way to remedy the situation when non-smuggled goods are detained. The meeting resolved that the industry association should provide proof to handle the matter. (4) The second item of the regulations on the transportation of domestic goods stipulates that domestic goods transported inland that do not pass through customs should be reported to the relevant industry association or chamber of commerce, which will issue a certificate of domestic goods. The chamber of commerce should draft a format and notify all industries to print it. The meeting resolved to hand it over to the secretary to draft. The meeting then adjourned. Furthermore, in order to prevent the transportation and sale of smuggled goods, the Ministry of Finance has stipulated that all relevant factories, businesses, transit companies, etc. must first register with the customs and obtain a license. When obtaining a license, the industry association or chamber of commerce must provide proof. In Shanghai, since the customs announcement, many have gone to register, but many have also neglected to do so. The regulations stipulated that applications for licenses must be made within twenty days of the local announcement. The announcement in this city was on June 23rd. After calculating the period, it will expire on the 11th of this month. Therefore, in recent days, there have been many requests to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and various industry associations for proof to obtain licenses. The workload of the chamber has increased significantly. Those who have not yet completed this procedure are also encouraged to complete it before the 11th of this month to avoid delays.
