The International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry sent letters to all national goods organizations in the city yesterday, stating: We previously received Instruction No. 44964 from the Ministry of Industry, based on Letter No. 713 from the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, regarding the Singapore Chinese Chamber of Commerce's request to establish a national goods introduction center in Singapore, instructing this bureau to consult with national goods manufacturers to carefully discuss and report back for approval. We copied the original request letter from the Singapore Chamber of Commerce and requested that you investigate and handle it. Many days have passed without a response. We are writing again to request that you promptly provide your opinions for submission to the ministry for approval.

Ministry of Communications International Radio Station Broadcasts Important Domestic News to Facilitate Reception in the United States: Advance Broadcast Starting on the 11th

The Ministry of Communications International Radio Station, in order to transmit domestic current events internationally, collects important news from various locations daily and broadcasts news telegrams via shortwave radio. Its messages are concise and rapid, and are highly regarded by various countries. It is now known that, in order to facilitate reception in the United States, the station will, starting on the 11th of this month, advance its broadcast to 00:30 midnight daily (16:30 Greenwich Mean Time). The call sign remains XGL, and the frequency is 797 OK0. The station has already submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications and consulted with the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to forward letters to various embassies and consulates abroad for notification.

Municipal Federation Petitions Ministry of Finance to Unify the Design of Legal Tender and Request Provision of Machinery for Self-Printing

The First Special District Citizens' Federation believes that since the Ministry of Finance implemented the legal tender policy, the original banknotes have been insufficient for circulation, leading to the alteration of various bank notes. The designs are not uniform, and authenticity is difficult to verify. The meeting resolved to petition the Ministry of Finance to reorganize and seek to print banknotes independently to recover profits. The original petition is recorded below: A petition is submitted for the matter of a petition. Since your ministry implemented the legal tender policy, it has received the support of friendly international nations and the endorsement of the domestic population. The financial market has been stabilized, and the industrial and commercial sectors have gradually improved. This is truly gratifying. However, with silver nationalized, circulation is limited to legal tender. Due to the complex issuance by the banking sector in the past, the banknotes used in the market are of various designs, presenting a chaotic and disorganized appearance. If counterfeit banknotes are mixed in by criminals, it is difficult to identify them. In addition, our country's banknotes have always been printed overseas, which is also a national loss. Therefore, the sixth executive committee of the association resolved: (1) to petition the Ministry of Finance to instruct the issuing banks to recall the old banknotes within a limited time; (2) to have the government raise funds to procure self-printing machinery to recover profits; (3) to centralize issuance with a uniform design and record it. It is reasonable to record this case and petition your ministry to separately review and implement it, which would be for the public good. Respectfully submitted.

Xu Chongqing and Others Departed for Guangdong Yesterday Afternoon; Yao Bolong, Huang Tianmin, and Others Traveled Together; Mayor Wu and Commander Yang Saw Them Off

According to the Central News Agency, the newly appointed Director of Education of Guangdong Province Xu Chongqing, Director of Guangzhou Navigation Administration Yao Bolong, Director of the Anti-Smoking Supervisory Office Huang Tianmin, Senior Staff Officer of the General Staff Headquarters Tang Tianxian, Senior Adjutant Ye Weiyu, Director of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau Cai Wuji, and others departed from Shanghai at 11:00 AM yesterday on the French postal ship Aramis, heading south to Guangdong. Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Secretary Geng Jiaji, Songhu Garrison Commander Yang Hu, Secretary Wang Zhinan, Dean of Academics of the Central Military Academy Yang Jie, and others went to the dock to see them off. The details of each situation are recorded as follows:

Xu Chongqing's Remarks

Before departing, Director of Education Xu Chongqing told a Central News Agency reporter that he had been ordered to go south. After arriving in Guangdong and meeting with Chairman Huang, he would determine the date of his inauguration. Director Wang Yingyu is currently in Nanjing, and his departure to Guangdong will be delayed by one trip.

Cai Wuji's Mission

Director of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau Cai Wuji, accompanied by Secretary Zhang Xiwu, departed from Shanghai for Hong Kong and then Guangzhou to handle the restoration of the Commodity Inspection Bureau. He is scheduled to stay in Guangdong for a month to complete his mission. Whether a branch bureau will be established in Shantou after the Guangdong bureau is restored is still pending a decision by the Ministry of Industry. It was rumored that Cai would be transferred to coordinate the Guangdong bureau, but Cai himself has denied this.

Huang Tianmin's Mission

The mission of Huang Tianmin, Director of the Anti-Smoking Supervisory Office, on this trip south is to establish an anti-smoking office in Guangdong. Therefore, after arriving in Guangdong, he will clean up the opium and drug trade in Guangdong based on the anti-smoking regulations promulgated by the Anti-Smoking General Supervision Department. As for Tang and Ye's trip south, it is said that this trip has no special mission.

Ju Zheng Arrives in Shanghai

Flying to Guangdong on the 11th; Chen Lifu to Travel Together

President of the Judicial Yuan Ju Zheng arrived in Shanghai at 7:15 AM yesterday morning on an overnight express train from Nanjing. After disembarking, he returned to his private residence in Wusong to rest. Chen Lifu, a member of the Standing Committee of the Central Party Headquarters, who is going to Guangdong to inspect and guide party affairs in Guangdong Province, is scheduled to come to Shanghai from Nanjing on the evening of the 8th and will also travel south on the same flight with Ju on the 11th.

Wenzhou and Taizhou New Rice Transported to Shanghai

Wenzhou and Taizhou in Zhejiang Province are famous early rice producing areas. This year, the early rice harvest in Wenzhou and Taizhou was abundant, and the new rice began to be harvested at the end of last month. The first batch of goods, totaling more than 600 dan, has been transported to Shanghai for sale. According to news from the rice market, since the end of the Dragon Boat Festival this year, the price of rice has fallen by more than three yuan per stone. Merchants have suffered losses. Recently, due to the busy farming season in the interior, the amount of river rice transported to Shanghai has decreased, and the market price has slightly rebounded by thirty cents.

Ministry of Communications Zhabei Long-Distance New Radio Station: Talking Last Night with Special Features and Improved Compared to Previous

According to the Daguang News Agency, after the installation of all new-style equipment at the Ministry of Communications Shanghai Telephone Bureau Zhabei Long-Distance New Radio Station was completed, continuous tests were conducted starting on the evening of the 4th of this month. The results of calls with domestic and foreign locations have been satisfactory. Yesterday morning, Director Xu visited the station for inspection. Then, engineers Yu and Huang, as well as branch chiefs Zhu and Fan, together with the resident supervisor, made preparations. The station was officially opened and put into use at 12:30 midnight yesterday, and call traffic was busy.

New Station Features: Connection and Contact

After the new long-distance telephone went into operation, the original old long-distance station was abolished. Because all the new station's sound receiving, speaking, and other equipment purchased from the United Kingdom are the latest models, the call traffic is greatly improved compared to the old station. From now on, the calls will have three special features: (1) The new station is equipped with a sound-amplifying pump telephone, which can increase the sound wave at any time when it is in use, which helps to lengthen the function of the radio wave. (2) The domestic long-distance lines and foreign lines that have been called are implemented through the same handover channel. The new station handles calls. (3) In the future, domestic and foreign calls at the new station, whether wired or wireless, can be directly connected, which can achieve the effect of receiving contact calls.

Chinese Settlement Calls: Four Connection Methods

The dialing method for calls at the new long-distance telephone station is as follows: Automatic machine users in the Chinese area who want to make domestic long-distance calls should first dial "40" and then call the other party's number (i.e., the called party). Concession users should first dial "02" to transfer to the long-distance station relay line to call. For foreign calls, concession users must dial "03." In the Chinese area, relay lines in Nanshi, Longhua, the city center area, and Zhenru transfer to the long-distance station to connect.

Installing Sound Amplifiers: Use Along the Line

In order to improve the call traffic between Beijing and Shanghai, the station, after the new long-distance telephone station was put into operation, specially selected and used booster motors along the Beijing-Shanghai route. The new telephone line between Beijing and Shanghai is laid along the highway, and the old line is laid along the railway. The two do not conflict.

Zhabei Public Station: Site Relocation

The Zhabei Telephone Branch recently submitted an application to the General Bureau, and it was approved by the technical meeting. The Zhabei public station that it set up will be moved to the "0" station to facilitate the concurrent management of night shift drivers.

Anhui Province Successfully Obtains Agricultural Warehouse Loan: Contract for 1 Million Silver Dollars Formally Signed; Agreement Reached with China Agricultural Bank and Bank of China for 3 Million Dollars

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, in order to relieve the rural areas, the Anhui Provincial Government is building warehouses and borrowing funds from the China Agricultural Cooperation Loan Syndicate and the China Farmers' Bank and Bank of China to handle agricultural storage, mortgage, transportation, and sales loans, totaling 4 million yuan. The 1 million yuan contract with the syndicate was signed on August 4. The 1.5 million yuan each with the China Farmers' Bank and Bank of China has also been agreed upon and contracts will be signed. The details are recorded below:

Building Warehouses

The Anhui Provincial Agricultural Administration Office was ordered to build provincial and county agricultural warehouses. (1) 22 provincial warehouses, in addition to handling storage and mortgage loans, also handle transportation and sales loans. Each warehouse can store 50,000 to 100,000 stones of rice and wheat. They will be fully completed before the end of September. (2) 96 county warehouses, specializing in storage and mortgage loans. Each warehouse can store 10,000 to 30,000 stones of rice and wheat. They will be fully completed before the end of August. Each provincial warehouse will have a certain provincial warehouse management office, and each county warehouse will have a certain county warehouse management committee, both of which will be guided by the Anhui Provincial Warehouse Management Office. This year, Anhui Province has had a bumper harvest of rice and wheat in various places, so all provincial and county warehouses are scheduled to open before the end of September.

Four Million Yuan

The Anhui Provincial Government borrowed a total of 4 million yuan from the China Agricultural Cooperation Loan Syndicate, the Bank of China, and the China Farmers' Bank to handle warehouse loans. The syndicate provided 1 million yuan, and the China Farmers' Bank and the Bank of China provided 1.5 million yuan each. The loan contract with the syndicate was signed on August 4. Lu Bochang, the syndicate representative carrying the contract, has already returned to Shanghai. The signatories were Yang Mianzhong, Director of Finance of Anhui Province, Liu Yiyan, Director of Construction, and Zou Bingwen, Li Zhongchu, and Wu Shangyuan, executive directors of the syndicate. The loan principles with the Bank of China and the China Farmers' Bank have also been agreed upon, and a contract has been drafted and will be formally signed soon. The methods are slightly the same as the syndicate's.

Original Text of Contract

The original text of the warehouse loan contract between Anhui Province and the syndicate is as follows: (1) When the agricultural warehouses guided and organized by the management office need storage and mortgage funds for handling storage and mortgage loans, the management office must first issue a formal introduction letter and send it to the syndicate for review. Only then will the syndicate allow the loan. (2) The total amount of this loan is temporarily limited to 1 million yuan. When the agricultural warehouse business is developed, the loan will be increased as appropriate. (3) The interest rate for this loan is set at 8.5% per month and calculated daily. (4) The term of this loan is from the date of signing the contract to March 31, 1937. Principal and interest will be settled together when due. (5) The investment area for this loan is in 24 counties including Fengyang, Nanling, Chaoxian, Wuwei, Wuhe, Lingbi, Qimen, Shitai, Yixian, Qide, Jixi, Xiuning, Langxi, Guangde, Ningguo, Jingxian, Taiping, Qingyang, Guichi, Tianchang, Lingjiao, Tai County, Fuyang, Wushan, etc., totaling eight provincial warehouses and fifty county warehouses. (6) This loan is specifically for the funds required by the agricultural warehouses listed in the previous article to handle storage and mortgage business and shall not be used for any other purpose. (7) The storage and mortgage loan methods for agricultural warehouses shall be formulated by the management office and the syndicate. (8) The syndicate allows each agricultural warehouse to advance 3,000 yuan for the provincial warehouse and 2,000 yuan for the county warehouse for the convenience of starting business. (9) All syndicate investments in storage and mortgage loans are based on agricultural warehouse storage certificates. The agricultural products stored by farmers are mortgaged at 70% of the current price. The agricultural products stored in each agricultural warehouse serve as the first guarantee for the syndicate loan, and the management office serves as the responsible guarantor for repayment. If it is found that there is a storage certificate without collateral, the management office shall bear full responsibility. (10) When the syndicate provides storage and sales loans, the syndicate shall handle all remittance transactions. (11) The storage loan period for each agricultural warehouse invested by the syndicate shall be up to ten months, but shall not exceed the period specified in Article 4 of this contract. (12) The syndicate has the right to audit the business and review the accounts of the agricultural warehouses that receive loans. The syndicate shall recommend four auditors, who shall be appointed by the management office. Their salaries and travel expenses shall be borne by the management office. (13) If there are any unfulfilled matters in this contract, they may be modified by both parties through consultation. (14) This contract is made in duplicate, with the management office and the syndicate each holding one copy as evidence. (15) This contract shall be submitted by the management office to the Anhui Provincial Government for approval and implementation. It shall take effect after both parties formally sign it.

National Goods Inspection and Promotion Group Scheduled to Depart from Shanghai

Three-Month Inspection Trip; National Goods Organizations Host Farewell Banquets

The Shanghai National Goods Movement Federation, in order to investigate the actual situation of national goods promotion in various places and the impact of smuggling, has specially formed a National Goods Inspection and Promotion Group along the Yangtze River. It has hired three ladies, Lin Kecong, Huang Bingpei, and Tao Xiaodong, to serve as members. The inspection period is set for three months, and they are scheduled to depart on the 20th of this month to carry out inspections in various provinces, including Beijing, Anhui, Hunan, Jiangxi, Henan, and Hubei, and to encourage women in various places to organize and wear national goods to promote the great work of advocating national goods in the women's community. The three ladies, Lin, Huang, and Tao, are currently preparing their luggage to depart as scheduled. Various national goods groups and women's organizations in the city are scheduled to host farewell banquets for the group in the coming days.

Four organizations, including the National Goods Maintenance Association, telegraphed the Central Government yesterday to request that Pan Gongzhan be confirmed as Director of the Social Affairs Bureau and petitioned the Mayor and Pan. Visiting the Mayor

At 11:00 AM yesterday, Wang Jiean of the China National Goods Maintenance Association, Shao Daren of the Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Goods, Hu Xiyuan (Xu Jianru, etc.) of the United Association of Machine-Made National Goods Factories, and Lu Xingzhuang of the United Association of National Goods Factories, visited the Mayor at the Municipal Government to request that Pan Gongzhan be confirmed as Director of the Social Affairs Bureau. They then congratulated Pan Gongzhan on his concurrent position as Director of the Social Affairs Bureau and requested that he not decline the concurrent position, so that he can use his expertise and meet the expectations of the public. In addition to expressing his gratitude, Pan said that he would handle the concurrent matter in accordance with the instructions of the Central Government in the future.

Four Organizations' Telegram

The four organizations jointly telegraphed the Executive Yuan yesterday, stating: Urgent, Presented to President Jiang of the Executive Yuan, Vice President Kong, We, the undersigned, hereby report that Mr. Wu Xingya, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau of this city, has been vacated due to illness. Mayor Wu has appointed Mr. Pan Gongzhan to act as Director, which is a cause for celebration for the industrial and commercial sectors. Mr. Pan previously served as Director of the Social Affairs Bureau and was known for his integrity and honesty. He handled matters in the industrial and commercial sectors with impartiality, peace, and clarity, and he has made special achievements in promoting the national goods movement. He is a rare and wise official in modern times. We earnestly request that you grant Mr. Pan's confirmation as Director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to showcase his talents and satisfy public expectations. We, the local officials, would not dare to interfere in the promotion of local officials. However, the factories under our jurisdiction have benefited greatly and have increased their enthusiasm for supporting wise officials. We earnestly request your clear understanding and approval. We are awaiting your orders with utmost urgency. China National Goods Maintenance Association, Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Goods, Shanghai United Association of Machine-Made National Goods Factories, Shanghai National Goods Factories United Association, respectfully bowed. Simultaneously, the Municipal Government was requested to immediately forward the request to the Central Government for appointment.

Various Associations' Telegram

The Shanghai Banking Industry Association, the Money Industry Association, the Electrical Manufacturing Industry Union, the Shipping Industry Union, and more than 100 other industry associations jointly telegraphed Chairman Lin of the National Government in Lushan and President Jiang of the Executive Yuan at 4:30 PM yesterday, requesting the immediate appointment of Pan Gongzhan as Director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. The general idea was that Pan had previously served as Director of the Social Affairs Bureau and spared no effort in industrial and commercial facilities. This time, the Mayor ordered him to temporarily act as Director, and he is familiar with the job. We are deeply delighted to have him, so please appoint him immediately to meet the expectations of the public.

Also, Three Trade Associations Cooperate in Investigating Smuggling

The Knitted Goods Trade Association, in order to assist the government in investigating smuggled goods, has resolved through its Executive Committee meeting to establish a Smuggling Investigation Committee. The committee consists of fifteen members: Gan Tinghui, Xia Yaoxi, Cai Yinqiao, Xu Wenzhao, Xu Xixing, Lu Renlin, Fei Xiangxue, Zhang Shaotang, Qian Jihua, Zhu Xinru, Zheng Hairuo, Xu Rongqing, Chen Hengrong, Zhang Lixing, and Chen Dafu. The first meeting was held yesterday. In addition to passing the articles of association, a notice was issued to the trade, the original text of which is as follows: "Our association, in order to assist the government in investigating smuggled goods, has organized a Smuggling Investigation Committee and commenced work. The following notices are hereby issued. We request all members of the trade (whether members or non-members) to pay close attention to the handling of matters: (1) All members of the trade must register with our association before the 12th of this month regarding the quantity and type of 'artificial silk,' 'artificial silk woven or interwoven products,' 'needles,' 'aniline dyes,' 'caustic soda,' and 'knitted piece goods' currently in stock (registration forms can be obtained from the association). Our association will forward this information to the Jianghai Customs for verification. (2) All factories must obtain tax payment certificates from the original sellers of artificial silk for the artificial silk currently in stock and keep them for inspection. (3) All factories purchasing artificial silk must obtain evidence of import tax payment given by the customs from the sellers of artificial silk and keep them for inspection. The customs will issue sales permits for the artificial silk fabrics reported by each factory based on the artificial silk tax payment evidence. (4) All factories must prepare Class A and B registration books for artificial silk and artificial silk woven or interwoven products in accordance with customs regulations, and record them at any time for inspection. These books have been printed by our association and can be purchased from the association. (5) When each factory applies to the customs for a license and requests the association to issue a certificate, it must fill out a letter of intent, pledging not to transport or sell smuggled goods, which must be signed by the person in charge and a reliable guarantor must be found. Approval will only be granted after the association has verified that there are no doubts. (6) In addition to recording the details of the purchase of artificial silk and the manufactured artificial silk fabrics in the books according to the regulations, each factory must also report to the association monthly in list form for verification by the customs. For other unclear procedures, you can come to the association at any time to inquire.

The Dried Seafood and Groceries Trade Association convened an executive supervisory committee meeting a few days ago, resolving to organize a Smuggling Investigation Committee. Fifteen members were elected: Ge Weian, Shao Baoxing, Zhou Lian Gui, Hua Nanshan, Wu Hankang, etc. Ge Weian was elected as the director and head of the general affairs group, Zhou Baochu was elected as the deputy leader, Dai Shanqing was elected as the leader of the investigation group, Wang Dachuan was elected as the deputy leader, Zhou Lian Gui was elected as the leader of the appraisal group, Chen Bingzhang was elected as the deputy leader, Hua Nanshan was elected as the leader of the public relations group, and Chen Lichen was elected as the deputy leader. The articles of association have been discussed and approved and submitted to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce's Smuggling Investigation Committee for record.

The Forwarding Trade Association organized and established a Smuggling Investigation Committee yesterday, resolving: (1) To elect Li Mulian, Zhou Renqing, Liu Chunlin, Shen Jusheng, Dong Zihua, Yu Xinchuan, Sheng Hanmin, etc., ten people as members of the Smuggling Investigation Committee, and report to the City Chamber of Commerce Smuggling Investigation Committee for record. (2) To jointly elect Liu Chunlin and Zheng Bochang as drafting members to formulate various rules and regulations. (3) To elect Dong Zihua as the head of the general affairs group, Shen Jusheng and Li Houzhai as the deputy leaders, Zhou Renqing as the head of the inspection group, and Yu Xinchuan and Shi Yinpu as the deputy leaders. (4) The smuggling investigation method will be stipulated in separate inspection rules. (5) The Smuggling Investigation Committee will use this association as its office location.

New British Military Commander Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

Brigadier General Simmonds, the newly appointed commander of the British Defense Forces stationed in Shanghai, arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM aboard the British mail ship Rajputana, accompanied by his wife. The outgoing commander, Brigadier General Charkey, and his staff boarded the ship to welcome them. They then disembarked together. It is reported that Brigadier General Simmonds has commanded the 157th Infantry Brigade for the past two years. He has achieved military merits in the European War and has been awarded several medals. This time, he came directly to Shanghai from England. A review of the troops stationed in Shanghai is scheduled to be held on the Bund on the 19th of this month. In addition to the British Lancashire Infantry, the American 4th Marine Regiment, the Japanese Marine Corps, French troops, and the Shanghai Volunteer Corps will all participate in the ceremony. The outgoing commander, Brigadier General Charkey, is scheduled to return to England on the Japanese Empress on the 23rd of this month. Charkey has been in office since 1933 and has made many friends in Shanghai. Now that he is about to leave, his colleagues are all saddened. Mayor Wu has specifically arranged a tea party at his private residence on Haig Road tomorrow afternoon to bid him farewell.

Guangdong Province Borrows Funds from Three Banks, Already Paid Directly by Guangdong Branches

Regarding the case of the Guangdong Provincial Government seeking 6 million yuan from the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, secured by the province's tax revenue, in order to consolidate finances, a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency continued to inquire with banking circles in Shanghai yesterday. It was learned that Song Ziliang, the special financial commissioner and director of finance of Guangdong, flew from Shanghai to Guangdong on the 22nd of last month. In light of Chen Jitang's departure with a large amount of savings and tax revenue, making consolidation difficult, he consulted with Zhou Shouliang, deputy director of the Business Bureau of the Central Bank, Bei Songsun, manager of the Shanghai branch of the Bank of China, and Tang Shoumin, general manager of the Bank of Communications, who had accompanied him. They negotiated a loan of 6 million yuan from the three banks, with 2.4 million yuan each from the Central Bank and the Bank of China, and 1.2 million yuan from the Bank of Communications, for the purpose of consolidating finances, secured by the province's tax revenue. At the end of last month, a contract was signed in Guangzhou with the Guangdong branches of the Bank of China and Bank of Communications. As for the Central Bank, it entrusted the Guangzhou branches of the Bank of China and Bank of Communications to handle the matter on its behalf. Now the funds have also been directly paid to the Guangdong Department of Finance by the branches of the Bank of China and Bank of Communications, so this loan is now a thing of the past.

Memorial Service Held Yesterday in Two Places for Wu Xingya

Colleagues from the Social Affairs Bureau

All colleagues of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau held a public memorial service for the former Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, Mr. Wu Xingya, at the bureau's auditorium yesterday at 1:00 PM. The details are recorded as follows: (1) Arrangement of the Memorial Hall: The memorial hall was set up on the north side of the auditorium. A portrait of former Director Wu was hung in the center. In front of the portrait was the sacrificial table, on which were placed fresh flowers, fresh fruits, and plain-colored incense candles. Bai Mao Sha Nan Gang Westward, Water Depth Reduced

Deep-Draft Vessels Take Note

Hydrographic Office of the Ministry of the Navy Notice to Mariners No. 184 states, "East Coast of the Republic of China, Yangtze River Estuary, Bai Mao Sha Nan Gang Westward, Water Depth Reduced":

Direction and Distance from the West Entrance Beacon of Bai Mao Sha

Depth

A 82 degrees, 4.00 nautical miles 29 feet (8.4 meters)

B 81 degrees, 3.86 nautical miles 30 feet (9.14 meters)

C 78 degrees, 3.75 nautical miles 27 feet (8.23 meters)

D 76 degrees, 3.51 nautical miles 28 feet (8.53 meters)

E 71 degrees, 3.45 nautical miles 26 feet (7.92 meters)

F 69 degrees, 3.15 nautical miles 26 feet (7.92 meters)

G 65 degrees, 3.25 nautical miles 20 feet (6.10 meters)

H 58 degrees, 3.00 nautical miles 22 feet (6.71 meters)

I 52 degrees, 2.95 nautical miles 20 feet (6.10 meters)

J 43 degrees, 2.92 nautical miles 18 feet (5.49 meters)

Location: Approximately 121 degrees 10 minutes East Longitude, 31 degrees 44 minutes North Latitude

Explanation: The water depth between the West Entrance Buoy of Bai Mao Sha Nan Gang and the Bai Mao He Buoy has reportedly decreased to the depths indicated for the above bearings. The depths are based on the latest Hydrographic Chart No. 141 of the Ministry of the Navy and have been corrected accordingly. Furthermore, the waterway is currently undergoing sounding, and further notices will be issued in the future. Mariners are advised to navigate with caution. Deep-draft vessels passing through this area must do so at high tide and exercise extra caution. Related charts: Hydrographic Chart No. 142 of the Ministry of the Navy. Reporting authority: Hydrographic Office of the Ministry of the Navy. Note: The bearings listed in this Notice to Mariners are calculated using true north as 0 degrees, rotating clockwise to 359 degrees. However, the directions of lights are calculated from the seaward direction. The range of lights is based on clear weather conditions. Fog signals are used only in foggy weather and will be further explained if necessary. The depths indicated are calculated using the datum of the largest scale chart. August 4, 1936.

Flying Flower Industry Representatives Travel from Beijing to Guling

The Shanghai Flying Flower Industry Association reports that the customs' prohibition of waste cotton exports has mistakenly included flying flower, refusing to declare and export them overseas. This has suddenly caused a halt to the bloodline, causing great panic among all the factories and merchants in the industry who are eagerly awaiting correction. Therefore, representatives Xie Zhongle and Bao Guoliang were sent to Beijing to petition the competent authorities. The representatives arrived in Beijing on the 6th and appealed to various ministries and departments. As a result, the situation of misunderstanding has been roughly clarified. However, as the responsible key personnel are all in Lushan, it is difficult to resolve the matter immediately. All have promised to immediately forward the matter for instructions. The representatives, in order to seek a swift resolution in view of the fact that the situation cannot tolerate a long period of delay, have already traveled to Guling to directly request the relevant personnel.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Drafts Revised Laws

The Business Committee and the Industrial and Commercial Laws and Regulations Committee organized by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, in order to improve the merchant organization and to suggest amendments to the Chamber of Commerce Law, appointed Pan Yangyao, Wang Xiaowen, Fang Jiaobo, Luo Qinghua, Xu Yongzuo, Lu Jiaqi, Yu Chengxiu and other seven people as drafting members of the revised Chamber of Commerce Law and the Industrial and Commercial Association Law. General Investigation of Smokers Ends Tomorrow, Public Security Bureau to Conduct General Verification, Although Staff Will Still Go Out to Investigate as Usual, More Than 12,000 Smokers Registered

According to the Dagong News Agency, the general investigation period for smokers in Shanghai will end tomorrow. Although today is a routine holiday on Sunday, all staff of the relevant departments of the Municipal Public Security Bureau are still going out to advise and investigate smokers who have quit, and conduct a general verification on schedule. The details are as follows:

End of Investigation Period

The Shanghai Municipal Government and the Special Commissioner's Office for Tobacco Suppression jointly issued a notice today, starting the general investigation of tobacco and drug suppression in Shanghai on May 10, and stipulating that the investigation will end on August 10. During this investigation period, the Municipal Public Security Bureau was ordered to supervise the sub-bureaus and districts to conduct serious investigations. It has been three months, and tomorrow (the 10th) is the end date of the general investigation. As to whether to extend it again, no order has been received yet.

Full Investigation

The Municipal Public Security Bureau, in view of the fact that the general investigation period is about to end, but for the sake of strict investigation, has ordered all staff of the relevant departments, together with all districts in the city, to go out to advise and implement investigations today, even though it is a routine Sunday holiday, so as to prevent unregistered smokers from escaping the net. Statistics show that since the beginning of the investigation period, the number of smokers who have registered has reached more than 13,200. On average, smokers in the Hubei-South and Zhabei districts account for four tenths.

Investigation and Punishment

The government's handling of the registration procedures for this investigation was originally to give smokers a final opportunity for self-renewal. Therefore, after the (1) voluntary, (2) compulsory, and (3) supplementary registration periods have passed, supplementary registration is still allowed, and no penalties or punishments are given. According to the bureau's regulations, after the end of the investigation period, if any unregistered smokers are found again, they will be sent to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for strict punishment in accordance with the Provisional Regulations on Tobacco Suppression and Punishment promulgated by the Military Affairs Commission, and no leniency will be shown.

General Verification

In order to thoroughly eliminate smokers, the Municipal Public Security Bureau will conduct a general verification on a regular basis after the end of this general investigation period for smokers who are sent to drug rehabilitation centers and various special hospitals for rehabilitation. The special hospitals are preparing to implement it simultaneously.

Special First District Court Trial Yesterday, Case of Counterfeiting Hubei Subsidiary Currency Bonds, Handwriting Authentication of Commission Letter, Liu Peiqing Temporarily Detained

Lu Fangzheng, a Hubei native and former doctor, previously forged a commission letter from the Hubei Provincial Bank and other documents, and printed 1.5 million of the bank's subsidiary currency bonds at the Huadong Engraving Company, located at No. 25, Maoyi Lane, 153 Meibai Road. On July 19, the first 50,000 yuan was printed and loaded onto the Ruichangwan ship. However, when passing through Xiaguan, Nanjing, it was seized by the Jianghai Customs, who recognized it as counterfeit and confiscated it. Lu also fled. Now, Liu Peiqing, the owner of Huadong Engraving Company, reported the matter to the Xinzha Patrol House, and the head of the patrol house ordered detectives to arrest Lu and send him to the Special First Court for interrogation and detention. This has already been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Tan Xinzhen continued the trial in the eighth criminal division. Attorney Zhang Tianyin of the patrol house clarified the case and stated that Liu Peiqing had also arrived in court today. Then, Mei Yu, a handwriting expert from the General Inspectorate of the General Patrol House, came to court to testify that the commission letter and other documents were written by one person, clearly indicating forgery. The patrol house also investigated the seizure of the 50,000 yuan subsidiary currency bonds with the Jianghai Customs. The Jianghai Customs sent a reply to the Nanjing Customs, stating that on July 19, three pieces of luggage were seized in the third-class cabin of the Ruiyangwan ship, containing four packages, which contained counterfeit subsidiary currency bonds with a face value of 50,000 yuan, and a seal of Jia Shiyi, the Director of the Hubei Department of Finance and the Manager of the Provincial Bank. The Hubei Provincial Bank also reportedly sent a telegram to the court, requesting a thorough investigation. Judge Tan summoned Liu Peiqing to court, questioned him, and, suspecting that Liu also had a significant connection to the crime, ordered Liu to be temporarily detained. The case was rescheduled for another hearing in seven days.

All Fish Products in This City to Be Concentrated in the Fish Market

An Additional Seat for Salted Fish Brokers to Be Added

The Shanghai Fish Market of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce is the primary marketplace for fish products in this city. Since the commencement of salted and dried fish transactions at the market on the 1st of this month, all fish product transactions in this city have been concentrated there. Daily business has been brisk. Due to the off-season for fresh fish, the total daily transaction volume, including salted and dried fish, has reached over 15,000 yuan. Fish shops that previously handled both fresh and salted/dried fish have already joined the market for transactions. In addition, Jie Shun and Yan Kang Fish Shops, which specialize in salted and dried fish, have been persuaded by market directors Tang Chengzong and Kui Yanfang to join the cooperative. They have agreed and requested to be appointed as market brokers. The market is considering this request and has agreed to add one seat, to be jointly held by the two shops. The two shops are currently in negotiations. The total number of market brokers was originally set at 4,000, which has already been fully subscribed by fresh and river fish shops. Due to practical needs, two brokers for seafood and jellyfish were previously added. The request from the salted fish shops will be submitted to the board of directors for approval, it is said.

Shanghai-Beiping Passenger Train Shortens Travel Time

Travel Time Reduced by Five Hours Compared to Previous Schedule; Effective from the 15th of This Month

The direct passenger train between Shanghai and Beiping will shorten its travel time. The Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai), Jinpu (Tianjin-Pukou), and Beining (Beijing-Shenyang) Railways have agreed that Train No. 301 will depart from Beiping at 6:00 PM daily, arriving at Shanghai North Station at 7:40 AM on the third day. Train No. 302 will depart from Shanghai North Station at 12:00 PM daily, arriving at Beiping at 1:55 PM on the third day. The travel time has been shortened by five hours compared to the previous schedule. The timetables for other trains on the Jinghu Railway will also be adjusted accordingly. The revised timetables have been drafted and are scheduled to take effect on the 15th of this month.

Small Foreman Zhang Honggao Crushed to Death by Boiler in Company Building on Rue Luban; Death Deemed Accidental; Favored Foreign Firm Provides Compensation

Zhang Honggao, a 27-year-old native of Qingjiang, worked as a small foreman in the machine engineering department of the French-owned Favored Foreign Firm. At 4:30 PM the day before yesterday, he led workers to the company building at 181 Rue Luban, intersection of Route Lafayette in the French Concession, to raise the water-cooled boiler that had been previously installed. Unexpectedly, the boiler, weighing approximately 2,600 pounds, shifted and toppled over as the workers were lifting one side due to the heavy weight. Zhang, who was standing nearby supervising, was crushed, sustaining injuries to his head and chest. He immediately lost consciousness. Efforts were made to lift him out and transport him to Guangci Hospital by car. However, he succumbed to his injuries en route and died. The body was then taken to the Tongren Foyuan branch mortuary for an autopsy. At noon yesterday, the French police reported the incident to Qiao Wanxuan, the Chief Prosecutor of the Second Special Court, who, along with a medical examiner, arrived at the mortuary to conduct an examination. It was determined that the death was caused by injuries sustained from being crushed. Zhang Zhoushi, the deceased's wife, was instructed to claim the body for burial. However, the deceased's family is poor. Friends and relatives raised funds for the funeral. The managers of Favored Foreign Firm, considering Zhang's tragic and accidental death, his young wife, and his young children, deemed it especially pitiable and agreed to provide a monthly allowance of 15 yuan for their sustenance.

French Concession Police Department Cracks Down On Indiscriminate Honking of Car Horns

Special Notice to Motor Vehicle Drivers: Strict Penalties for Violations

The Police Department of the French Concession has issued a special notice regarding the crackdown on indiscriminate honking of car horns: "Notice is hereby given: Article 36 of the current Traffic Regulations of the French Concession stipulates that the use of car horns must be appropriate. In particular, indiscriminate honking is prohibited in residential areas and at night. All drivers traveling on roads within the Concession must take note of this." According to the spirit of this article: (1) Horns should be used briefly and concisely. (2) Except in situations of danger, "such as warning moving vehicles," drivers of parked vehicles are strictly prohibited from indiscriminate honking. All motor vehicle drivers are hereby notified. The penalties for violating this regulation have been determined. In addition to fines and prosecution, drivers found guilty will also have their licenses suspended. The Commissioner of the Police Department urges all motor vehicle drivers to pay attention. Especially

Severe Penalties will be imposed in the following situations where indiscriminate honking occurs: (1) Between the hours of 11:00 PM and 6:00 AM, particularly in residential areas; (2) When a vehicle is following a line of cars that are moving slowly or stopped to avoid obstacles or obey the instructions of a police officer; (3) To attract the attention of traffic police managing traffic lights, with the intention of proceeding ahead of others; (4) On roads, at intersections, or other locations where slow driving is required, with the intention of passing freely; (5) To attract the attention of: 1. People leaving theaters, cinemas, or amusement parks who need transportation; 2. People coming out of private residences or large buildings. All are expected to comply with this notice. Commissioner Fevrier.

Rickshaw Pullers Association Holds Joint Meeting Yesterday

Dispatching Personnel for Inspection to Intensify Work

The Shanghai Rickshaw Pullers Association convened a joint meeting of station chiefs, service personnel, and puller representatives at 627 Fangbang Road at 5:00 PM yesterday, presided over by Zhang Zhenshan. Matters decided upon: (1) In response to the recent frequent thefts of rickshaws, which cause great distress to the pullers, the following was resolved regarding how to strictly prevent such incidents: (A) A letter will be sent to the authorities requesting the investigation and arrest of these thieves. (B) All service stations will be instructed to provide immediate protection and attention. (C) A rickshaw insurance department will be established. (2) Regarding improving the attire of rickshaw pullers, it was resolved to send a letter to rickshaw vendors requesting: (A) Raincoats be provided on rainy days. (B) Overcoats be provided in winter. (C) Straw hats and necessary preventative medicines be provided in summer. (3) Regarding intensifying the work of service stations, it was resolved that: A. Personnel will be dispatched to inspect the service provided at each station. B. Medical treatment and medicine will be administered, entrusted to the management of each station. C. Inflation and tire repair services will be implemented for the convenience of pullers. The rest is omitted.

Police Chief Testifies in Court

Yang Fuqing, a native of Taizhou, runs a wine shop at 3 Binde Lane, Qiujiang Hostel, 44 North Fourth Road, Hongkou. He is accused of secretly operating an illicit establishment where women are induced to engage in "mirror polishing" (a euphemism for prostitution). The case was discovered by the Inspection Department of the Public Security Bureau, who arrested Yang and confiscated rubber implements, forwarding him to the District Court on charges of obscenity. Yesterday, Judge Chen Kangsun opened the hearing. Yang Fuqing testified that he was 32 years old and had been running the wine shop since June 1st, only for half a month. He employed four female waitresses: Zhang Gendi, Jin Abao, Ni Fengying, and Zhang Abao. He denied operating a "mirror polishing" ring. When questioned about the evidence found, he replied that he was framed during an argument with Inspection Department personnel. At this point, Liang Zhangyou, the police chief of the Qiujiang Road Police Station, testified that the case was reported by Chen Sizhou, who led him and police officers to investigate. They saw rubber implements on the table downstairs, and six women and Yang Fuqing were present. They were all taken to the station. The arrest was carried out by investigators from the Special Affairs Section of the Public Security Bureau, based on instructions from our officer Ouyang Wei. He stated that we were following orders and were completely unaware of the details of the case. At this point, the judge adjourned the case for further questioning at a later date.

Wei Xudong Invents Chemical Steaming of Ramie for Textile Production

Ramie textile is one of the main textile industries and is relied upon as a raw material for modern military supplies. Everything from daily necessities such as towels, drapes, blankets, clothing, etc., to materials such as airplane wings, parachute fabrics, belts, and fire hoses, is made from ramie fabrics. However, ramie textile production in China is still in its infancy, and we rely heavily on imports, resulting in alarming financial losses year after year. Mr. Wei Xudong, recognizing this problem, carefully considered it, researched it meticulously, and spent four years developing a method for chemical steaming of ramie and cotton, which can be spun into counts as fine as 180 (its raw ramie material comes from provinces such as Jiangxi, Hunan, and Sichuan, which are exceptionally abundant). The results are better than or equal to imported products. This has been jointly certified by spinning mills such as Shenxin, Yongan, Anle, Xiefeng, and Dingxin, as well as the China National Products Maintenance Association, the China Underwear Dyeing and Weaving Factory, and others. However, due to financial difficulties, a factory has not yet been established for production. Apart from speculative ventures, capitalists in general are mostly uninvolved with domestic product production, which benefits society and the country. Therefore, Mr. Wei, after inventing the ramie textile method and exhausting his energy and resources over several years, remains determined and refuses to be discouraged. However, his personal financial resources are running out. He has therefore submitted a request to the National Economic Council of the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry and other high-level government agencies, requesting funding to establish a factory for production to benefit the people and stop financial losses. He has also submitted samples, certificates, and business plans as evidence.

Xu Wancheng's Bail Issue

Suffering Greatly in Detention

Xu Wancheng has been detained for over two months for commenting on the theft of new-style handguns at the Shanghai District Court, etc. It is said that he is living in very poor conditions, suffering from ulcers on his feet, and his heart condition has also worsened, with occasional vomiting of blood and extreme suffering. Cai Yuanpei, Jiang Kanghu, Wang Bocai, Huang Jingwan, Wu Zhiqian, and dozens of others have requested the court to uphold justice and grant bail in accordance with the law, but to no avail. Based on legal principles, even if Xu is found guilty of both charges of obstructing official duties and defamation, the heaviest combined penalty would be a fine of only 1,100 yuan. A request for bail in this amount has been denied. Lawyers Wu Linkun and Ding Zheming have filed an appeal, and the High Court has ruled to overturn the District Court's denial of bail. A written request has been made to handle the matter fairly and expeditiously grant bail, but after half a month, there has been no response. It is said that enthusiastic members of the city's educational circles will make a second joint petition.

Soliciting Collaboration for Music Textbooks

The songs published by the Numing Society aim to arouse the spirit of national struggle. Now, Shanghai Municipal Shagang Elementary School (Pudong) requires the publication of two kinds of music textbooks. However, the songs in them are not those already published by the Society, but are all self-selected song titles such as "Watching the Sunrise, Praise of Sleep, Lullaby, Qing Tian Bai Ri Man Di Hong (Blue Sky, White Sun, and a Wholly Red Earth), The Moon Shines White, Happiness Like Gods in Heaven, Seeking Brother Song, March of the Volunteers, Qing Tian Bai Ri Song, March of the Army, Wild Goose, Bread." Therefore, the typesetting fee is over ten yuan, and the number of copies is only 80. The cost of paper (wood paper), printing, and binding is at least sixteen yuan (two jiao per copy). As for the students of the school, they can only afford one jiao at most. The Society is limited by funds and is in a dilemma. Therefore, it intends to seek cooperation with other schools, so that the more copies are printed, the lighter the cost will be, and the general children can afford it. If there are schools willing to adopt this as a music textbook, they can contact the Society at 132 Fangxie Road, Ximen.

Chen Jianmin to Go to Europe

Mental science is the latest scientific invention of modern times. Its application can not only treat diseases and change the character, but also assist education and medicine. It can also train military and police, and contribute to the country. A certain cultural organization in this city is now planning to establish a special lecture on mental training, and intends to send mental science expert Chen Jianmin on a special trip to Germany and Austria for investigation, so as to learn from it. It is said that as soon as Chen agrees, he will be scheduled to go to the West.

Who is the "Red Pill King" After All? Qian Zupei or Qian Guodong? Reopened Debate Concludes Again

Qian Zupei, known as "Little Shandong" and the "Red Pill King," was previously arrested by the French police and handed over to the First Special Court in November 1932 for selling Lu Changfa's No. 11 Red Pills throughout the country and making a considerable profit. During the investigation, he was released on bail of 8,000 yuan in cash and then fled back to his hometown. Subsequently, the court ruled to confiscate his bail money and issued an arrest warrant. For four years, until recently, the French police discovered that Qian had secretly come to Shanghai and, together with the Laoza Gate police, arrested Qian at the Central Tea House on Guangxi Road and handed him over to the Second Special Court. The Police Department filed a public prosecution in accordance with the law. The case had already been tried and was scheduled for sentencing. However, the presiding judge, believing that the case still needed further investigation, ordered the cancellation of the closing arguments. All this has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhang Chaozuo presided over a hearing in the First Criminal Court to interrogate Qian. Qian claimed that when he was arrested in 1932, he was summoned to the court, not arrested. He was questioned again, and Detective Fang Guilin, who handled the case, was summoned to testify. Fang testified that when he initially arrested Shi Yinbao, Wang Agen, and other red pill sellers, they claimed that their boss was Qian Guodong, known as "Little Shandong." Since Qian was well-known in Ruifuli, he went to arrest him. Without questioning him, he first handed him over to the court and then waited for further investigation. Unexpectedly, Qian escaped after being released on bail. Therefore, the police did not take a detailed statement from Qian at the time. Qian was questioned again, and the court ordered the closure of the arguments and scheduled the verdict for the 13th. The defendant remained in custody.

Taicang Robbery Case: Jiang Axiao Extradited from Shanghai

Defendant Denies Robbery

On the night of the 27th of last month, eight bandits broke into the home of Xiao Fuxiang, a resident of Caijiawan, Taicang. Four of the bandits, armed with handguns, threatened the victims to remain silent and robbed them of cash, banknotes, and jewelry worth 2,000 yuan. They fled through the door. The incident was reported to the local Public Security Bureau, requesting an arrest. The day before yesterday, Squad Leader Wang Yuqi and Detective Cai Fuquan learned from an elderly Tongzhou native named Wang Zhangkun that his nephew, Jiang Axiao, a Tongzhou native, had recently visited relatives in Maojia Town, Taicang, and was suspected of being involved in the case. Jiang lived in an unnumbered bungalow on Gaolang Bridge in Shanghai. Wang and the detective traveled to Shanghai overnight and requested the Yulin Road Police Station to assist in the arrest. Chinese Detective Zhao Baosheng was dispatched and arrested Jiang near Huade Road, taking him into custody. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Lawyer Zhang Shizhu of the Municipal Council explained the previous circumstances, stating that Jiang Axiao claimed at the police station that he had recently moved to 101 Dean Lane, Taopeng Road, and denied any involvement in the Taicang robbery case. It was confirmed that 101 Taopeng Road was where he had moved from Gaolang Bridge on the 6th of last month. Cai Fuquan, a detective from the Taicang Public Security Bureau, then presented an account of the incident. Jiang Axiao firmly denied the charges. Judge Xiao ruled to remand him in custody and issue a formal extradition letter.

Liang, a Monk, Electrocuted

Liang, a monk, a 28-year-old Ningbo native and worker at the Jiangnan Shipyard in Gaochang Temple, Nanshi, was accidentally electrocuted at 8:30 PM last night. Another worker rescued him, and he was immediately taken to Shanghai Hospital for treatment by car. However, he succumbed to his injuries en route and died.

Zhenbei District Farmers Association Provides Medical Treatment

In view of the fact that the summer sun is scorching and diseases are prone to occur, the Zhenbei District Farmers Association, in the past month, hired Chinese and Western doctors Lu Xinyun, Shen Wenbin, Xu Dingren, etc., to organize a summer free clinic at the association's location in Gongxing Bridge, Xibaoxing Road. They are on duty to provide medical treatment every day, giving medicine to the needy. For the few days it has been open, the number of patients coming to the clinic from nearby has been quite crowded, reaching over 300 people. The funds for the free clinic are sometimes stretched. It is said that each director has been trying to raise funds.

Shengtai Cigarette Paper Store's Sheng Ada: Adopted Daughter Enticed Away, Investigation Reveals, A Letter Found in Xingzhen's Chest, Xiang Sanbin Admits Without Hesitation

Sheng Ada, the owner of the Shengtai cigarette paper store at 457 Bo Shi Road in the French Concession, a local resident, is fifty years old. He used to be a houseboy and in the twelfth year of the Republic (1923), he adopted a daughter named Xingzhen, who is now sixteen years old. She received elementary education and is of ordinary appearance. She usually helps with household chores and store affairs at home. Unexpectedly, at 3:00 PM on the 6th of this month, she suddenly disappeared without a trace. After reporting to the French Police, Sheng searched her belongings at home and found a love letter from someone in Xingzhen's chest. The original text reads, "Time flies like an arrow; six and a half months have passed in a flash. During this process, I feel very bored, but when I think carefully, there is endless happiness in sight. Calculating the days, our time is coming soon. Please be very secretive in everything. If you have anything, bring it when you have the chance. Please cherish money, we will need money soon, so don't waste it. I hope you take care of your health. I think of you when I lie in bed, and I wait on the balcony in the morning to see you open the door. I am very happy to see your beautiful figure. Please don't miss me. Goodbye, [Day], Love, [Sender]." Sheng then presented the letter to the police and requested an investigation. After investigation by detectives Jin Bingwen and Li Dedong, it was learned that Xiang Sanbao from Wuxi, who worked at the Xiesheng Fruit Store at 479 nearby, was suspected of abduction. Xiang was arrested and confessed to enticing Xingzhen and hiding her in Room 140 of the Mantingfang Yuelai Hotel, where they had intercourse once. Thereupon, detectives Jin and Li, together with the French police, went to the address and rescued the girl, bringing her back to the police station for her family to take home. Yesterday, Xiang was sent to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special Court. The prosecutor of the police department requested an extension of the investigation and then filed a complaint for trial. Judge Zhang Chaozuo reported to the authorities, stating that the case concerned public morals and forbade public attendance. After questioning the defendant and the victim, he ordered a postponement for further questioning on the 12th. The defendant was remanded in custody, and Xingzhen was ordered to be examined by the forensic department.

Lost Property Found on Zhabei Public Bus, Handed Over to the Police for Disposal

The Shanghai Huashang Public Bus Company collects items left on the bus by passengers and brings them back to the company to await the owner's claim. Lost property is frequently found throughout the year. Apart from those that have been claimed, there are still items that have been accumulated for more than a year. To fulfill its responsibilities, the company has listed the items and sent them directly to the North Station Public Security Bureau for disposal to comply with procedures. The list of lost items includes: nine pieces of clothing, four pairs of shoes, eighteen purses, 499 copper coins, three umbrellas, and twenty other items, totaling fifty-four items.

Police Chief Yu Uncovers Den of Pen Thieves, Education Director Xu Loses Pen, Stolen Pens and Pawn Tickets Recovered

Education Director Xu of the Central Military Academy encountered a thieving gang yesterday while passing near the Xinkaihe area on the Mingguo Road. They stole a fountain pen worth tens of dollars. Director Xu, recognizing the thief's extraordinary skills, telegraphed Police Chief Cai of the Public Security Bureau to request an investigation. Chief Cai immediately instructed Yu Pu, the chief of the Yemiao Police Station, to dispatch detective Wang Guilin. Wang uncovered a den of fountain pen thieves at No. 1, Lane 24, Gaodun Road in the Lao Beidou police precinct. The suspects, Xu Aben, 36 years old, from Shanghai, Zhang Guiting, 36 years old, from Sichuan, and Ma Xiangji, 40 years old, from Sichuan, were apprehended. Two fountain pens and a pawn ticket were also recovered. They were immediately taken to the police station. It was not immediately known if the pens were the original stolen from Director Xu. They were sent to the headquarters for interrogation.

Banking Sector Mediates Credit Bureau Strife, Settlement Agreed Upon Last Night, To Be Implemented After Submission to Board of Directors for Approval, All Employees to Resume Work Tomorrow

After the sudden joint strike of all employees of the China Credit Bureau on Yuanmingyuan Road on the 7th, bank representatives such as Kong Shouheng mediated tirelessly. Finally, at 5:00 PM yesterday, both parties reached a settlement. All employees are scheduled to resume work tomorrow. The details, as investigated by a Dagongshe reporter, are as follows:

Mediation Process

Since the outbreak of the joint employee strike, representatives from various banks, including Shanghai Commercial Bank, Xinhua Xingye Bank, China Bank, and Overseas Chinese Bank, went to the bureau to convene a meeting with all employees to conduct mediation. However, due to the wide divergence of opinions between the two sides, the meeting ended without any result. Subsequently, Kong Shouheng, the deputy manager of Zhejiang Industrial Bank, continued to be responsible for mediation. The employees immediately selected Li Baimeng, Yao Dayan, Shen Zhijing, and three others as representatives. As a result of mutual consultation, Mr. Kong presented the conditions proposed by the employees to the board of directors for consideration and implementation in order to resolve this dispute as soon as possible.

Terms Agreed Upon

The conditions proposed by the employees have been agreed upon in principle and will be submitted to the board of directors for approval today before implementation. They include: (1) The four unpublished resolutions will be marked as "canceled" on the public announcement board, and signed and sealed by the secretary. (2) Ni Tongjia and Pan Jingfang are required to resign voluntarily, and the board of directors will not retain them. (3) The powers of Secretary Ge Buliang will be restored. (4) Mr. Kong expressed that he can take full responsibility for reporting to the board of directors on the issue of concrete guarantees for the occupational safety of all employees, and notify that the regulations for guaranteeing the occupations of colleagues are included in the personnel management rules. (5) The board of directors will dispel the unfavorable political rumors about the bureau from the outside world. With regards to the three colleagues Ji, Tong, and Qian, who are related to the attachment, those who voluntarily resign should be given six months' severance pay. The demands of the printing workers will be handled by the director of administrative affairs authorized by the board of directors.

Resumption of Work Tomorrow Morning

Since the principles of the settlement were agreed upon, the employees elected five temporary representatives last night to remain at the bureau today, awaiting the notice from the board of directors. Once they are satisfied, the representatives will immediately notify all employees and workers to resume work on Monday.

Philanthropic Road Morgue: Two Bodies Examined Yesterday

One is Le Bao Bao, Burned, One is Wang Zixiang, Hanged

Le Liu, a 28-year-old woman from Yancheng residing at No. 116, Lane 149, Moganshan Road, was sleeping in a small room above the kitchen stove in the house with her four-year-old son, Bao Bao, last night. Unexpectedly, at around 1:00 AM this morning, the bed curtains suddenly caught fire, burning the woman and the child. Fortunately, it was discovered early, preventing a widespread fire. When the fire brigade arrived after receiving the alarm, the fire had already been extinguished. After receiving the report, the Putuo Road Police Station ordered detectives to investigate. It was learned that a candle had been lit beside the bed where the woman was sleeping. It was possibly played with by the child, causing it to fall onto the curtain. The woman and her son were sent to Guangren Hospital for treatment. The woman only suffered minor burns on her arms, so she left the hospital after being bandaged and medicated. However, the child, due to his young age and more severe injuries, could not be saved and soon died. Wang Zixiang, a 23-year-old man from Shaoxing, was originally an assistant in the kitchen of the Danghu Hotel at No. 9, Shanxi Road. Recently, due to extreme financial difficulties, he had a sudden suicidal thought. He went to Room 27, which was specially set aside by the hotel, and hanged himself while no one was paying attention. At around 1:00 PM, the tea attendant discovered him and quickly tried to untie him, but he was already barely breathing. The local Lao Zha Police Station was notified, and an ambulance was called to the scene. He was rushed to Renji Hospital, but treatment was ineffective, and he soon died. The above two bodies were both taken to the Philanthropic Road Morgue by the respective police stations. Yesterday morning, Song Genshan, the prosecutor of the First Special Court, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan, clerk Wang Zuyi, and others, arrived at the morgue to examine the bodies and confirm their identities. They then ordered the respective families to sign statements and claim the bodies for burial.

Public Concession Industrial Accidents in July

The Shanghai Municipal Council Factory Inspection Department reported that a total of 229 industrial and occupational accidents occurred in the Public Concession in July, resulting in 12 deaths and 7 injuries to women, one of whom died. The causes of 212 accidents were generally clear, and preventive and remedial measures were investigated and instructed in 113 cases. In terms of the type of industry, machinery and hardware manufacturing still accounted for the highest number of accidents, with a total of 51 accidents and 2 deaths. This was followed by the transportation industry with 35 accidents, the construction industry with 32 accidents, including 1 death, the textile industry with 28 accidents, including 2 deaths, the food and tobacco manufacturing industry with 21 accidents, including 2 deaths, and the leather industry with 5 accidents, including 2 deaths. In terms of the causes, 48 accidents were related to electricity, including 1 death, 7 people were injured by electric shock, including 2 deaths, 7 people were injured by explosions, including 2 deaths, 13 people were burned by molten metal, 35 people were injured by falling from heights, including 3 deaths, and 28 people were injured by falling objects, but there were no fatalities.

Shanghai Municipal Council Police Department Orders Crackdown on Street Prostitutes, Yesterday's Letter Responds to City Federation's Inquiry

The First Special District Citizens' Federation previously received reports from the Hubei Road, Edward Road, and other district branches that every evening, as the lights came on, prostitutes lined the streets, forcibly pulling pedestrians, preventing merchants and residents from moving forward. Yesterday, the Police Department replied with a letter stating, "In response to your letter of August 6th regarding the crackdown on street prostitutes, we have received it. We have already ordered the relevant authorities to investigate and handle the matter. We hereby reply to inform you accordingly."

Ministry of Finance Rejects Request for Reduction of Raw Material Import Tax for Enamel Industry

The Shanghai Enamel Industry Trade Association, citing the sluggish market and declining business, presented a request to the Ministry of Finance last month to approve a reduction in the import tax on various raw materials to maintain the industry. Yesterday, the association received a reply from the Ministry of Finance stating, "We have received your submission regarding the request to reduce the import tax on various raw materials used in enamelware to reduce costs and maintain the industry due to poor business conditions. After the Ministry referred the matter to the National Tariff Commission for investigation, it was found that the current tax rates on various foreign raw materials used in the manufacture of enamelware are not high compared to the general import tax rates for raw materials. Therefore, your request to reduce the import tax on various raw materials used in enamelware cannot be approved. As for the refund of raw material taxes on enamelware sold abroad, there are also many obstacles. However, the Ministry has recently promulgated the Regulations on Customs Warehouses for Manufactured Goods and ordered the Jianghai Customs to conduct a pilot program. The customs warehouse system is designed to facilitate various manufacturing industries that use imported raw materials and promote foreign trade. You should order the industry to organize enamelware manufacturing institutions and apply directly to the Jianghai Customs for processing to reduce costs and facilitate exports. You are hereby informed."

Native Cloth Industry Requests Exemption from Native Cloth Tax in Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian Regions

The Shanghai Native Cloth Industry Association submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, asking that the Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian unified tax bureaus be instructed to abolish the supplementary tax on handmade native cloth. The submission states: "Regarding the request for your ministry to order the Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian regional unified tax bureaus to abolish the supplementary tax on handmade native cloth to maintain the established case. The national government decided in 1927 to exempt domestic handmade native cloth from tax, referring to the established case of 1918 and explicitly ordering the exemption. The reason for this exemption was that the national government, considering that both the supply and demand sides were poor people, exempted the tax before the abolition of the likin tax to promote domestic products. In 1930, when the cotton yarn unified tax was established, customs export tax receipts were required for verification. However, these native cloth weavers are all poor people with limited purchasing power. Merchants collect small amounts and consolidate them into large quantities, so how can they obtain tax receipts for verification? Based on the principle of one tax per item, the tax has already been levied at the source. Moreover, since there is an explicit order for exemption, there should be no doubt about levying the tax again. The association, based on these reasons, has made detailed submissions. Subsequently, your ministry approved and ordered the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui unified tax bureaus to issue special "transportation joint soil" certificates, allowing tax-free export. In the same year, Liaoning Province forcibly levied a supplementary tax, detaining goods and harassing merchants. The association again submitted a request to stop this, and your ministry ordered the Liaoning Provincial Department of Finance to forward the order to return the detained goods and exempt the tax. Historically, the three northeastern provinces have been the main sales area for this native cloth. Now, Guangdong and Guangxi have become the sole sales area, although they are less than three-tenths of the three provinces. However, on the shipping route, there is an opportunity to indirectly extend it to foreign countries. This year, the Dutch East Indies authorities have set import restrictions. The association wrote to the Shanghai International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, requesting that it send letters to foreign ambassadors and consular commercial officers, asking the Dutch East Indies authorities to exempt Chinese native cloth from import restrictions. The Trade Bureau also submitted a request to the Ministry, asking the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to forward an order for negotiations. The reply from the Dutch authorities indicates that there is room for change. Therefore, the association joined the Nanyang Industrial Investigation Group organized with the assistance of the Ministry of Industry, selecting merchants familiar with foreign conditions to act as representatives for investigation, hoping to achieve satisfactory production and sales cooperation. Furthermore, in this extravagant era, with other goods filling the market, the local people in various provinces and overseas Chinese are happy to purchase this native cloth because it is durable and of better quality than other goods. This is not only the case, but the people's patriotism is also the effect of the government's tax exemption and promotion. The association only seeks to reduce costs by one point, which can increase sales by one point, as an aid to rural areas. Recently, the Ministry of Industry sent personnel to Shanghai to gather opinions from manufacturers to promote domestic cloth. The association has already sent sample cloths to the Ministry of Industry for review. Furthermore, the supplementary tax levied in Guangdong Province can still be recovered for machine-made products in Shanghai, but this native cloth has a "tax-free independent transportation special certificate" that clearly states that the tax cannot be refunded. In this regard, native cloth is subject to a heavy tax due to the tax exemption. Considering this matter repeatedly and considering it in light of the principle of one tax per item, it seems that this supplementary tax should not be levied. Moreover, the native cloth business tax in various provinces and cities has therefore been uniformly exempted. In the past, it was possible to speak of self-government in the provinces, but today, when your ministry orders the Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian regional unified tax bureaus to reorganize tax collection, all seven types of goods, including cotton yarn, which have already paid the unified tax, must not be taxed again to comply with the principle of one tax per item. At this time when all merchants are celebrating, if the association remains silent, it will not only fail in its duties, but also fail to live up to our government's repeated orders to promote domestic products and attach importance to rural areas. I hereby respectfully state that the handmade native cloth, which has been explicitly exempted from tax, has already paid the tax before it becomes a woven product. Due to the above reasons, the cotton products directly produced from cotton yarn do not have tax receipts for verification. Your ministry approved and ordered the issuance of special "soil" transportation joint certificates, which cannot be refunded. For several years, the association has been silently suffering a heavy tax. We are restating the reasons again to provide for your consideration. We respectfully request that your ministry review and verify the established case of exempting handmade native cloth from tax, and order the Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian regional unified tax bureaus to abolish the supplementary unified tax and the Guangxi military donation bureau's military donations. We respectfully wish the Ministry of Finance of the National Government on behalf of tens of thousands of weavers and poor people. Attached are one copy each of the supplementary tax bill from Guangdong Province and the military donation bill from Guangxi Province, as well as two original transportation joint certificates. Shanghai Native Cloth Industry Association."

Bicycle Rental and Manufacturing Associations Hold Joint Meeting Yesterday

The Shanghai Bicycle Rental and Repair Industry Association and the Bicycle Manufacturing Industry Association held a joint meeting at Ren'an Lane, Guling Road, last night. More than 30 people attended, including representatives from Tongchang, Deli, Runda, Li Xiaoshi, and Han Baotai. Li Xiaoshi chaired the meeting, and the following resolutions were made: (1) To avoid outsiders falsely claiming to be wholesalers, the bicycle repair association will issue sales certificates to its members. They must have the certificate to sell, otherwise they will not be entitled to this right. (2) Standardize market prices, and the door-to-door price list should be the same. Any members who do not sell at the market price will be punished according to the rules once discovered. (3) Reorganize the membership roster for verification purposes.

Wang Xun Calligraphy School Offers Calligraphy Samples

Complete Set for One Dollar and Ten Cents, Requester Must Send Handwritten Letter

Wang Xun Calligraphy School, located at No. 8, Dingji Lane, East Entrance of Avenue Joffre, Shanghai, specializes in teaching calligraphy techniques with rapid progress. Over the years, it has been praised in the art world and is highly reputable. By practicing according to the methods, you can achieve mastery. The entire set only costs one dollar and ten cents for paper and postage.
